Nwomasua Soafoɔ a wahyehyɛ ne Member a ɔwɔ Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu ama Assin South Rev . John Wm Fordjour ama akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ awerɛhyem sɛ wɔn ahiadeɛ ho hia aban paa.
Sɛnea ɔkyerɛ no, nhyehyɛeɛ a wɔayɛ ne sɛ wɔbɛto Ɔkyerɛkyerɛfo Welfare App akasa akyerɛ akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ a wɔn asɛm yɛ mmɔbɔ.
Akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ abadiakyire a wayiyi nsɛm ano no yɛ asɛnhia ma aban na ɔhyɛ bɔ sɛ ɔbɛma sukuuni biara a n’adwene si no pi wɔ nsɛm bi a ɛbɛma ɔkyerɛkyerɛfo no anya nkɔsoɔ, ɔhaw ne nneɛma foforo a ɛhia sɛ ɔka ho.
“Sɛnea wobetumi de wɔn ho ahyɛ akyerɛkyerɛfo nsɛm mu fee mu no, Adi . Fordjour ada no adi sɛ wɔn a wɔhwɛ di nsɛm no ho dwuma no afono wɔn wɔ ɔmantam biara mu sɛ akyerɛkyerɛfo a wɔn ho akokwaw wɔ mmɔden a wɔbɔ sɛ wɔbɛma wɔn asetra atu mpɔn no mu.
Nwomasua Soafoɔ panin, Dr. Yaw Osei Adutwum, ahwɛ kwan sɛ ɔbɛboa ama ɔhaw pii a ɛwɔ akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ ne wɔn adwuma mu no akɔ fam.
Berɛ a ɔne nsɛmtwerɛfoɔ rekasa wɔ Ghana Akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ Fekuwɛ (GNAT) a ɛwɔ Nkranhodie a ɔgyinaa sukuu no ananmu wɔ Nkran no, John Ntim Fordjour hyɛɛ ɔkyerɛkyerɛfoɔ no sɛ ɔmfa ne ho nto aban so na ama watumi anya ɔhaw a ɛwɔ ɔman yi mu no ano aduru.
Na dwumadie a wɔde sika hyɛɛ adwuma mu no nso wɔ asɛmti yi so: “Beyond Teachers Fund; Making the Teacher Economund.”
Ɔrekasa atia akanni ne GNAT no, ɔkaa no pen sɛ akyerɛkyerɛfo a wɔwɔ ɔman no mu nyinaa aboa kɛse ama ɔman no sikasɛm anya nkɔso. Ɔhyɛɛ aban bɔ sɛ ɔbɛma akyerɛkyerɛfo ahu nneɛma a ehia wɔn wɔ bere a ɛsɛ mu.
N'ani gyei sɛ GNAT yɛɛ nhyehyɛe pa a mfaso wɔ so a GNAT yɛe wɔ wɔn kasa mu na ama emufo asetra atu mpɔn. Ɔkamfoo GNAT nnwuma a na nnipa pii yɛ wɔ Unique Insurance ne Ghana Aduruyɛ Ayaresabea no nso. Ɔkamfoo GNAT nso sɛ ɔde ne sika hyɛɛ adwuma no mu, na ɔde ne sika no kɔhyɛɛ nnwumakuo ahodoɔ no mu.
Abenfo Fordjour maa akyerɛkyerɛfo no awerɛhyem sɛ, Nhomasua Asoɛe no bɛma akyerɛkyerɛfo 280,000 kwan ma wɔayɛ nhyehyɛe a ɛbɛma wɔatumi de sika a ne bo yɛ den ama wɔn na wɔatumi aboa wɔn yiye.
Ɔfrɛɛ akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ a wɔwɔ ɔman yi mu nyinaa sɛ wɔmfa wɔn ho nhyɛ Nhomasua Asoeɛ mu na wɔntoa so nhyɛ wiase nhomasua nhyehyɛeɛ mu.

Yei sii wɔ Yawda da a ɛtɔ so dunnum no. Sɛnea ahɔho no kyerɛ no, na ahintasɛm no yɛ nhyira a efi anyame no hɔ.

“Yɛwɔ adwuma sɛ yɛbɛyɛ wɔ Ajumako Ochiso Community a ɛwɔ ha no mu, enti ɛbɛboa yɛn ma yɛatumi de sika ahwɛ yɛn mma nhomasua ne fie nnwuma so. Yei nti yɛfrɛ atumfoɔ sɛ wɔmmra mmɛboa yɛn mma yensiesie nsɛnnennen a yɛrehyia wɔ Ajumako Ochiso ne Community dwumadie mu no

Wɔn a wɔabɔ wɔn sobo no dɔɔso
Aban no atu akɔtra Burkinabe nnwontofo a wɔwɔ Ghana ntua ase bere a ɛrebɔ amanneɛ sɛ wɔresisi adan wɔ Bawku na ama wɔanya ahobammɔ kɛse wɔ ɔman no fã hɔ no
Ɔmanpanin Akufo-Addo de too dwa sɛ dapɛn baako akyi no, aban no yɛɛ ahwɛyiye paa sɛ wɔbɛto ahyɛ asoafoɔ a wɔwɔ Burkina Faso no so.
Ná ɔne Bawku Naba rekasa wɔ nhyiam bi ase sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a ɔbɛtu kwan akɔ Atifi fam atɔe mantam mu.
“Nea ɛkwan a mo mantam yi wɔ sɛ mobɛdi dwuma wɔ Burkina Faso no ma ɛda adi pefee sɛ saa awudifo ne nsɛmmɔnedifo a wɔpɛ sɛ wɔpa yɛn nkwa wɔ Ghana no.

“Mmara no mu ɔha mu nkyem aduonum ka sɛ wɔpɛ sɛ wotu kwan kɔ ɔman foforo so, nanso ɔha mu 11 na wɔbɛtena ɔman no mu anaa wobefi hɔ. Nhwehwɛmu no kaa sɛ, wɔn a wɔyɛɛ saa no mu fã kɛse no ara de nnuan a ɛyɛ ahabammono, nhomasua ne asetra mu gyinapɛn pa gyinaa nea enti a wofii ɔman no mu bere a biribi sii no.”
Nhwehwɛmu no daa no adi sɛ, “Nea wɔn a wobisabisaa wɔn nsɛm no ɔha mu 80 na wɔsusu sɛ wɔn ani da so wɔ Ghana ho wɔ mfe 20 a ɛreba no mu. Bɛboro mfe du mu no, wɔn a wɔyɛɛ wɔn adwene sɛ wɔbɛnya nkɔsoɔ wɔ ɔman no mu daakye ne hokwan ahorow.

Asuae a Ɛhwɛ Sikasɛm ne Asomdwoe Ho Nsɛm So (IEP) ho nsɛm so no ama Ghana ne ɔman a asomdwoe wom sen biara wɔ Afrika wɔ Mauritius wɔ afe 2021 mu .
Wiase Nyinaa Asomdwoeɛ Abɛdwadie no ne wiase nyinaa asomdwoeɛ nhyehyɛeɛ no. Abɛdwadie yi gyina amantam ne nsasesin 163 a wɔn ankasa pɛ asomdwoeɛ so. Amanneɛbɔ yi kyerɛ sɛ saa amanneɛbɔ yi gyina nsɛm a ɛfa asomdwoeɛ ho a ɛtɔ asom, sikasɛm ne ɔkwan a wɔbɛfa so anya asomdwoeɛ amammuo.
Abɛdwadifoɔ bosome mu no, Ghana bosome dumiɛnsa a ɛmu yɛ dummiɛnsa a ɛmu yɛ dummiɛnsa a ɛmu yɛ dummiɛnsa a ɛmu yɛ dummiɛnsa
Mauritius yɛ ɔman a asomdwoe wom sen biara wɔ Afrika, na nnipa a wɔwɔ wiase nyinaa dodow si 28, na Botswana nso kodii mprɛnsa wɔ Afrika ne 41 wɔ wiase nyinaa. Oduu Nigeria no, na wadi mfe 146 wɔ Togo, Uganda, The Republic of Congo ne Cameroon.
Iceland da so ara yɛ ɔman a asomdwoe wom sen biara wɔ wiase, baabi a yɛatena fi afe 2008 no. Abɛka ho wɔ New Zealand, Denmark, Portugal, ne Slovenia mantam mu.
Afghanistan yɛ ɔman a asomdwoe nnim koraa wɔ wiase yi mu afe a ɛto so anan mu, na Yemen, Syria, South Sudan, ne Iraq. Burkina Faso yɛɛ nhwehwɛmu wɔ Global Peace Index 2021 mu.
Sɛnea amanneɛbɔ no kyerɛ no, nnipa a wɔwɔ Sub - Sahara Afrika no mu fã hyiaa basabasayɛ nnansa yi ara. Wɔn a wɔte Namibia no nyaa basabasayɛ a ɛsen biara wɔ wiase nyinaa no mu ɔha biara mu 6.
Kesee fam Sudan da so ara yɛ ɔman a asomdwoe nnim koraa wɔ ɔmantam no mu, na aman a asomdwoe nni mu wɔ wiase nyinaa no mu biako wɔ asomdwoeɛ mu wɔ afe 2021 mu.
Ɔman biara mu no, asomdwoeɛ a ɛresɛe kɛseɛ wɔ Burkina Faso no nso ne ɔman biara mu. Aban no sii gyinaeɛ sɛ ɔbɛdi adwadifoɔ ne ahamufoɔ a wɔdi adwamansɛm wɔ ne manfoɔ ako atia adowa no.
Amanneɛbɔ no sii so dua sɛ ɔman mu basabasayɛ kɔɔ soro ɔha biara mu nkyem 10 wɔ wiase nyinaa, na abrannaa a ɛwɔ hɔ no yɛ 14,871 basabasayɛ, ɔyɛkyerɛ ne atuatew a wɔayɛ ho kyerɛwtohɔ wɔ wiase nyinaa wɔ afe 2020 mu.
Amanneɛbɔ no kae sɛ Covid yɛ " tumi a ɔde di dwuma wɔ amanyɔsɛm ne ɔman mu basabasayɛ mu daakye. Ɛde kaa ho sɛ, saa ɔhaw yi betumi ama sikasɛm mu ahokyere ne sikasɛm mu ahokyere ano abrɛ ase. Ɔman no betumi
Eyi nyinaa akyi no, nnipa a wɔwɔ wiase nyinaa adwumayɛbea abiɛsa te nka sɛ wɔwɔ ahobammɔ anaa ahobammɔ wɔ hɔ nnɛ sen mfe anum a atwam no. Ebinom ayɛ nhwehwɛmu ahu sɛ efi afe 2008 reba no, awudisɛm anya nkɔanim kɛse, na aman 123 ahu sɛ efi afe 2008 reba no, awudisɛm adɔɔso.
Nsɛmma nhoma no daa no adi nso sɛ, “anyɛ yiye koraa no, wiase nyinaa asomdwoeɛ 0.07 bɛkɔ so asɛe wɔ 2021 Global Peace Index mu. Ɛwom sɛ wiase nyinaa asɛe kakra de, nanso eyi ne nea ɛto so akron wɔ mfe 13 a atwam no mu a wiase nyinaa asomdwoe asɛe”
Amanneɛbɔ no de kaa ho sɛ, " afe a etwaam no, aman 87 yɛɛ nhyehyɛe pa bi ho kyerɛwtohɔ wɔ asomdwoe mu, bere a aman 73 yɛɛ ɔsɛe ho kyerɛwtohɔ no. Aman abiɛsa nso yɛɛ nsakrae biara wɔ wɔn sikasɛm mu. Ɔmanpanin abɛdiakyire Nana Addo Dankwa Akufo-Addo ama Ghanafoɔ anya awerɛhyem sɛ wɔbɛnya nkɔsoɔ wɔ n'atirimɔden mu.
Sɛnea ɔkyerɛ no, mfe anan a edi hɔ no betumi anya Ghanani biara asetra so nkɛntɛnso pa.
“Medwene ho yie araa ma mfeɛ nan a ɛdi hɔ no bɛnya nkɔsoɔ wɔ Ghana manfoɔ abrabɔ mu.” Ɔtitenpɔn no kaa asɛm no berɛ a na ɔretu anamɔn akɔ Nigeria na watu abadiakyire no.
Owura Akufo-Addo rekasa akyerɛ Addo a ɔda Imo Man no ano wɔ Nigeria Owelle Rochas Anayo Okorocha, Dwoda de kaa ho sɛ: " Ghana sikasɛm agye ntini wɔ mfe abiɛsa anaa anan a atwam yi mu nanso yɛde nteɛso ne ahyɛde a emu yɛ den na ama yɛatumi de ɔman no asan adi yiye”
Ɔmampanyin panin a ɔhwe Ɔmanpanin, John Dramani Mahama wɔ abatoɔ a ɛtwa toɔ mu no rebɛba Nigeria abɛdiakyire a ɔne fango kannifo, Muhammudu Buhari bɛbɔ ho nkɔmmɔ.
Owura Akufo-Addo maa Imo State amrado no awerɛhyem nso sɛ, sɛ ɔne Afrika Atɔeɛ aman mmienu no ntam yɛ papa a, ɔbɛhyɛ mu den.
“Yei boɔ a adwadie a ɛda aman mmienu no ntam no som bo. Ɛho hia sɛ nkitahodie a ɛte saa kɔ so wɔ yɛn manfoɔ ne yɛn akannifo ntam. Wɔde ahotosoɔ ma yɛn manfoɔ sɛ yɛrebɔ mmɔden asiesie wɔn haw na yɛaboa wɔn ama wɔn asetena ayɛ den. Nanso aman mmienu yi mu deɛ, ɛyɛ papa sɛ Afrika Atɔeɛ ne asasepɔn no bɛbu so.”
Ɔmanpanin John Dramani Mahama asi so dua sɛ Joseph Whittal yɛ Ɔsoafo foforo ma Hokwan a Nnipa Wɔ ne Atɛntrenee (CHRAJ).
Ná Owura Whittal ani abere rehwɛ dwumadie bi so wɔ Flagstaff House Benada awia.
Owura Whittal ayɛ adwuma sɛ CHRAJ nanmusini firisɛ Ɔmanpanin yii ɔsoafoɔ panin, Lauretta Vivian Lamptey sika firiiɛ.
Ɔmanpanin apaw Ms . Josephine Nkrumah sɛ Ɔman Asoɛe a Ɛhwɛ Amammerɛ So (NCCE) no titrani abadiakyiri .
Ms. Nkrumah a ɔyɛ aban dwumayɛni abadiakyiri wɔ dwumadie no mu no sii Owurayere Charlotte Osei ananmu sɛ ɔsoafoɔ panin wɔ ɔman no mu.

GN Health Insurance Company Ltd, Groupe Nduom nnwuma 75 no mu baako afi ase reyɛ adwuma wɔ Ambulance Services wɔ Ghana.
Wɔhwɛ kwan sɛ wɔbɛyɛ nnwuma foforo a egye ntɛmpɛ wɔ aduruyɛ mu na wɔde ahwɛ wɔn a wɔwɔ ayarehwɛ a egye ntɛmpɛ no.
GN Health Ambulance Adwuma no nso de nnɔnhwerew 24 bɛyɛ ayaresa ne ahude a aba so yi ho mmuae.
GN Health Issah Adam guamtenani no hyɛɛ no nsow sɛ, “once Ɔmampanyin ne CEO a ɔwɔ Groupe Nduom Nduom, Dr Papa Kwesi Nduom, ne Senior Vice manpanin, Owurayere Yvonne Nduom ne Directorfoɔ nyinaa reboa ama Gupro nnwuma atu mpɔn.”
Ɔka kyerɛɛ apɔmuden adwumayɛfoɔ nhyiamu no sɛ, “Sɛnea ɛda nsow wɔ Groupe Nduom Nduom Ndufra Nduraho mu no, wɔde saa Ambulance Adwuma yi reboa adwumayɛfoɔ a wɔwɔ Nkran ne Mfinimfi Mantam mu.”
Sɛnea akontaabu kyerɛ no, nnipa bɛboro ɔha biara mu 60 a wowuwui wɔ Ghana no yɛ nea wɔnam ambulance adwuma so betumi de mmea a wɔwɔ labour ne akwanhyia akɔ ayaresabea a ɛfata. Experts gye di sɛ, tebea a ɛde owu ba no betumi ayɛ nea ɛfata, te sɛ nea GN Health Ambulance Adwuma hwehwɛ sɛ wɔyɛ wɔ bere a ɛsɛ mu no.
" Apɔmuden bɛtumi ahwɛ ahu sɛ yɛatete EMTs (Emergency Medical Technicia) ne Ambulance Drivers a wɔnim adeɛ pɔtee a ɛsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ wɔ tebea a egye ntɛmpɛ mu.
“Nnipa a wɔde ambulance yɛ 350 no wɔ nnɛyi nnwinnade ne nneɛma a wɔde di dwuma a ɛho hia ma tebea horow a egye ntɛmpɛ ne ɔhwɛ a wɔde ma ayarefo. Mesrɛ sɛ monhyɛ no nsow sɛ ɛnyɛ saa nneɛma yi nko na wɔde retu kwan a ebetumi ahwɛ ayarefo.”
Ambulancefo wɔ mfiri a wɔde yɛ adwuma ansa na wɔahwɛ wɔn ho yare. Wɔde nnwinnade a ɛho hia na ama wɔatumi ayɛ mfiri ahorow pii, efi ahomegu mfiri ne mfiri a wɔde yɛ adwuma so kosi nneɛma nketenkete so, na wɔde boa wɔn a wɔmmrɛ wɔn ho ase no ma wotumi de yɛ nneɛma nketenkete.
Aban ahyɛ bɔ sɛ wɔbɛsɔ wɔn a mframa bɔne atoto wɔn wɔ Okuturukubɔ mu wɔ La no ahwɛ.

Akraman akɛse a wɔregye n'ahengua no nso apirapira dedaw. Ɛyɛ den ma wɔn sɛ wɔbɛyɛ Gbese hene.
Mmea baanu wuwui, na afoforo bɛboro 12 nso pirapirae, bere a kar bi yerae wɔ Daboya - Busunu kwan a ɛda Northern Northern Mantam mu no so, na polisifo asi so dua wɔ Tuesday anwummere.
Ná kar no wɔ nnipa 14 a wɔde wɔn rekɔ Daboya fi Sawla kɔ Nkramofo ayeforohyia bi ase.
West Gonja mantam mu polisi panyin ASP Seidu Weh kae sɛ kar no nɔma yɛ AS 2304 - 15 bere a woduu kurow bi a ɛbɛn Daboya mu mpofirim no , na wokunkum nnipa baanu no ntɛm ara .
Ná nea wawu no yɛ aberewa a wadi fi mfe 42 kosi 45.
Ɛwɔ hɔ ara a wontumi nhu nea ɛmaa asiane no bae nanso sɛnea ASP Seidu kyerɛ no, polisifo bɛhwehwɛ ofirikafo no adwene mu ahwɛ sɛ ebia mmosa bi wom anaa.
Ɔde wɔn a wɔapirapira no mu dodow no ara kɔɔ amantam ayaresabea a ɛwɔ Tamale no, na wɔn mu baako pɛ na wɔsa no wɔ Damongo.
Daboya-Busunu kwan no so da mpan ɛmfa ho sɛ ɛyɛ hu no.
Ɔmanfo no ampene amanneɛbɔ yi so sɛ ɛno ne bere a edi kan wɔ afe no mu wɔ akwanhyia bi mu.
Wɔka sɛ akwanhyia pii to ntwa.
Asoeɛ soafoɔ, Dr Matthew Opoku Prempeh, aka sɛ Aban no reyɛ adwuma de reboa Ghana aban no ma watu ne ho ahyɛ mfiridwuma mu dwumadie a ɛho tew na wotumi de ho to so, te sɛ nuklea ne
Ɔkaa sɛ anyinam ahoɔden ne galamsey wɔ dwuma titiriw bi a ɛboa ma anyinam ahoɔden nhama yow wɔ mfiridwuma mu.
“Yɛhwɛ kwan sɛ anyinam ahoɔden mfiri bɛkɔ so anya nkɔanim kɛse, nuklea ahoɔden ahoɔden fã titiriw a ɛwɔ hɔ nnɛ no nso ne ahoɔden a ɛso sen biara a ɛma anyinam ahoɔden nhama a ɛwɔ fam no nya nkɔanim wɔ sikasɛm mu, na ɛma carbon awo ntoatoaso a ɛwɔ fam no ɔha biara mu nkyem 40.”
Ɔtwee adwene sii Amanaman Ntam Adwumayɛkuw bi a ɛde anyinam ahoɔden yɛ adwuma so sɛ, sɛ wɔamfa nuklea ahoɔden anni dwuma a, ebetumi ayɛ den ama wɔn sɛ wɔbɛkora wɔn ahoɔden so.
Dr Opoku Prempeh kaa saa asɛm yi wɔ kasa bi a wɔkenkan ma n’adiakyire wɔ Ghana Nuclear Power Programme a ɛwɔ Nkran mu.
Wɔ asɛmti no ase: “Nuclear Energy Innovations: The Future Technologies for Clean Energy ne ɔkwan a wɔfa so ka Ghana anyinam ahoɔden afiri afiri mu", Ghana Industries (AGI), ne Ghana Nucle Power (NPPPP) no na ɛmaa ho kwan.
Dr Opoku Prempeh hyɛɛ no nsow sɛ, sɛ wɔdan kɔ anyinam ahoɔden nhama so a, ɛbɛma anyinam ahoɔden afiri nso asɛe nneɛma foforo te sɛ kar, ne nneɛma foforo a atwa yɛn ho ahyia a ɛsɛe mframa.
Ɔkaa sɛ, " “Within Ghana awo ntoatoaso a ɛwɔ tumi yi mu, nsɛmnsɛm a ɛfa nkɔsoɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ obi nya, sika a ɔde bɛtɔ, sika a ne bo yɛ den, ne ahoɔden a ɔde bɛdi dwuma, ne mansotwe de ɔhaw aba abɛɛfo adwadie so”
Ɔkaa sɛ, sɛ ɔman no hia anyinam ahoɔden, nneɛma a ne bo yɛ den, ne nneɛma foforo a ɛfa nuklea ahoɔden ho a, ebetumi ama wɔanya saa tumi no bi.
" Nuklea anyinam ahoɔden afiri a wɔde di dwuma foforo no mfa carbon anyinam ahoɔden nhama nnyɛ adwuma, na mmom ɛma wonya mfaso kɛse wɔ nsakraeɛ yi mu, adansie ne mfeɛ 60 a ɛtwa toɔ no mu.
Ɔkaee sɛ afe 2007 mu no, kan Ɔmanpanin John Agyekum Kufuor hyehyɛɛ boayikuw bi a Ɔbenfo Daniel Adzei-Bekoe panin de too dwa sɛ Ghana bɛtumi de anyinam ahoɔden ayɛ adwuma sɛ afiri a wɔde yɛ adwuma.
Saa bere yi nyinaa na Ghana wɔ ahoɔden.
Ɔkyerɛɛ mu sɛ, nea ɛbɛyɛ na ɔman no anya nkɔanim wɔ mfiridwuma mu nkɔso mu no, na aban no aboa ama ɔman no ahoɔden atu mpɔn na ama amanfoɔ anya kɛtɛasehyɛ ne sika a wɔde bɛyɛ nuklea ahoɔden nhyehyɛeɛ.
Eyi ama NPG no abɛyɛ Ghana nuklea ahoɔden afiri a edi kan no wura.
Ɔkaa sɛ, Owura Fred Oware a ɔyɛ adwuma wɔ NPG Board no de n’adwene sii nneɛma a ɛho hia paa so sɛ ɛbɛma ɔman no anya fahodie na wahyehyɛ mmara a ɛfa nuklea akodeyɛ ne nnwuma a ɛbɛkɔ so wɔ ɔman yi mu nyinaa
Nuklea anyinam ahoɔden ho adwuma akyi no, Ɔman Soafoɔ no kae sɛ, ebetumi ama wɔn a wɔwɔ nuklea mfiri te sɛ afiri ketewaa bi a wɔde yɛ adwuma no anya anyinam ahoɔden a ɛbɛma wɔn a wɔyɛ adwuma wɔ po so hyɛn mu no ho atɔ wɔn.
" “Nuclear mfiridwuma mu nimdeɛ reboa nnipa wɔ akwan foforo pii so, na ɛreboa ma nneɛma akɔ so yiye”
" Mfiridwuma, mfiridwuma ne mfiridwuma mu nimdeɛ a wɔde yɛ adwuma wɔ nuklea ho nimdeɛ mu no di dwuma wɔ wiase nyinaa, a Ghana nso ka ho.
Efi bere a wɔhyɛɛ ase yie wɔ bɛyɛ mfeɛ anan a atwam ni no, towtua ho nhyehyɛe a ɛwɔ hɔ no abɛyɛ nea mfaso wɔ so.
Efi afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu nsia a ɛtwa toɔ mu no, wɔn dodow kɔɔ soro koduu ɔpepem 38.5 afe a edi hɔ no, na ɔpepem 70.2 wɔ 2020 mu, na wɔn a wɔhwɛ dwumadie yi so no dodow si ɔpepem 90 wɔ afe 2021 mu.
Ghana Revenue Authority (GRA) kae nso sɛ ɛyɛ aduan ne Beverages Association of Ghana (FABAG) ne wɔn a wɔyɛ adwuma wɔ ɔman no mu no na wɔde retua wɔn ka wɔ nneɛma a wɔkora so wɔ mmeae a wɔkora nnuan
Ghana adwumakuo a wɔtintim nwoma, Buck Press, ne wɔn a wɔka ne ho, DelaRue, a ɛyɛ adwumakuo a wɔyɛ adwuma wɔ Britain no na ɛyɛ wɔn asɛyɛde sɛ wɔtintim ttamtamtam no ma GRA, berɛ a Streamline Resources a ɛwɔ Tema Porto no, boa nnwumakuo ahodoɔ no a wɔnni mfiridwuma ho nimdeɛ.
Ɔsoafoɔ panin a ɔwɔ Adwadifoɔ Tax Stamp a ɛwɔ GRA, Owura Kwabena Apau Awuah Awua Anto, a ɔkyerɛɛ saa kwan yi no kaa sɛ, adwamansɛm ne atirimɔdensɛm a ɛwɔ afɛfɛdeɛ ne afɛfɛfɛsɛm mu no bɛtew ɛdɛfɛfɛfɛfɛfɛfɛfɛ
Ɔrekasa wɔ tablɛt a ɛwɔ Tema Porto mu no, Akuo bi a wofi Graphic Communications Group Limited (GCL) ano Yawda a etwa to mu no, Owura Anto kae sɛ, GRA Mmarahyɛbɛdwani no de krataa ama adwadifoɔ 34 ne wɔn adwadifoɔ a wɔn ho yɛ den no, a wɔn adwuma ka ho.
GGCL bɔɔlbɔ kuw a Managing Director, Owura Ato Afful kaa wɔn a ɔda Daily Graphic ano, Owura Kobby Asmah; Director, Marketing, Owura Franklin Sowa, ne Editor a ɔwɔ The Mirror, Msreen Hand.
Na kuw no wɔ Tema sɛ wɔn ani sɔ nkɔsoɔ a ɛwɔ towtua nhyehyɛeɛ mu no, na wɔne GRA nso ayɛ nhyehyɛe a ɛbɛma wɔatumi atu anammɔn yie.
Owura Anto kaa sɛ adwadie nhyehyɛeɛ no bɛtew adwadie so na ahwɛ ahu sɛ nneɛma pa nkutoo na ɛbɛma ɔmanfoɔ anya akwahosan ne ahobammɔ.
Saa ara nso na ɔkaa sɛ, nhyehyɛeɛ no bɛhwɛ ama wɔn a wɔdi adwadifoɔ ne wɔn a wɔyɛ fagudeɛtubea yi ho dwuma no akɔsi akan wɔ kwan a wɔfa so tua tow a ɛfata so.
Owura Anto kae sɛ: “What yɛ adwuma wɔ Tema adan ne nnwumayɛbea ahodoɔ 13 wɔ ɔman no mu baabiara a yɛwɔ adwadie a yɛde yɛ adwuma no boɔ yɛ den.”
Ɔkaa sɛ, berɛ a ɔrehwɛ dan no so no, ɔbɔɔ ka bi te sɛ bɔɔlbɔ, aneneɛ, ɛlɛtrɔnik sika ne nneɛma bi te sɛ anwa a wɔde twitwi fam.
Ɔdaa no adi sɛ berɛ a adwuma no kɔɔ so wɔ afe 2018 mu no, aban no sii gyinae sɛ ɔde abosome nsia bɛma wɔn a wɔbɛtumi de atua ka no, nanso ankosi saa da no ara na Ɔsahene no retwe wɔn a wɔhwɛ dua no so no aso sɛ wɔde sika no bɛma wɔn.
Owura Anto kaa sɛ, saa nhyehyɛeɛ yi bɛkyerɛ sɛ GRA boɔ no bɛkɔ fam, anaa ɛbɛbɔ ka no bi.
“Yɛ aman te sɛ Kenya, adwadifoɔ tua wɔn ka anaa wɔnya nneɛma no bi wɔ po so hyɛn gyinabea hɔ.
Ghana nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛfa towtua nhyehyɛeɛ ho no de asodi no ato adwadifoɔ anaa adwadifoɔ so.
Owura Anto kaa sɛ, “Amanfoɔ a wɔyɛ adwuma wɔ aman pii so no wɔ nnwumayɛbea ahodoɔ wɔ nnwumayɛbea ahodoɔ.”
Wɔ nsɛnnennen a wohyiae nnansa yi a wohui sɛ wɔatwentwɛn wɔn nan ase wɔ aperententu no ho no, Owura Anto kyerɛkyerɛɛ mu sɛ ɛnyɛ ahyɛnsode no nti na wɔyɛɛ saa, na mmom nnipa a ɛtɔ mmere bi a na wɔde wɔn ho hyem no.
Nanso ɔka kyerɛɛ wɔn sɛ, wɔn a wɔde wɔn sika hyɛ adwuma mu kɛse no bɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛkwati ɛka a wɔbɔe wɔ sika a wɔde bɔɔ ka no ho, a mpɛn pii no, wɔde wɔn nneɛma no kɔɔ dan no mu sɛ wɔmfa nsi dan no mu, tebea a ɛma wɔtwentwɛn wɔn nan ase no.
Saa ara nso na bere a ɔsesaa n’adwumam dwumadie no, ɔhaw a ɛwom no maa ɔtwentwɛnee ne nan ase.
Nanso, mfiridwuma ho animdefo yɛɛ adwuma wɔ mfiri no so sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wobetumi ayiyi ade foforo no.
Wɔ ne kasa mu no, Owura Asmah frɛɛ GRA sɛ ɔmmma sukuu no nnyɛ den mma dwumadie a wɔde baa aguadibea hɔ bere ne bere mu no.
Ɔkaa sɛ ɛhia sɛ wɔsua nwoma kɔ akyiri, efisɛ ɛbɛhwɛ sɛ ɛbɛkɔ so pɛpɛɛpɛ, na ɛbɛhwɛ nso sɛ nnipa ntena nhyehyɛeɛ no mu.
Ɔkamfoo GRA mpanyimfo ne adwuma sohwɛfo, Streamline Resources sɛ watu anammɔn a ɔde bedi ɔhaw no ho dwuma.
Ɔkyerɛɛ mu sɛ GCGL no ne GRA bɛbom ayɛ n’ahobrɛdie no ho adwuma awieɛ, berɛ a ɔhunuu mfasoɔ a ɛwɔ towtua nhyehyɛeɛ mu no.
“Megye di sɛ GCGL ne GRA wɔ berɛ a ɛfata sɛ wɔnya berɛ ma ɔmanfoɔ ate asɛm no, na ama yɛatumi atɔ biribi afiri nnipa hɔ” Owura Asmah kaa sɛ.
Adwadie Asuaeɛ (IES) aka sɛ pɛtro boɔ a ɛmu yɛ den bɛbue kwan mu. Asɛm bi a IES de too dwa no daa no adi sɛ pɛtro bo a ɛwɔ ɔman no mpomma mu no kɔɔ soro.
Wɔ June 2021 mfɛnsere a edi kan mu no, fango nnwumakuw a wɔyɛ fango (OMCs) no mu fã kɛse no ara bo kɔɔ soro ɔha biara mu 3% wɔ fango ho. Based wɔ saa nkɔanim yi mu, sɛ wɔkyekyem pɛpɛɛpɛ a, fango bo kɔ soro ba fam wɔ GHS597 wɔ galine ne galine mu.
Sen Petroleum, Benab Oil, Cash Oil, Goodness Oil, Top Oil ne Frimps Oil, nom fango kakra wɔ mpɔtam hɔ.
Wɔ mfɛnsere no mu no, sɛ wɔkyekyɛm pɛpɛɛpɛ a, amanaman ntam benchmark Brent de $73.98, a egyina hɔ ma ɔha mu nkyem 4.05 fi mfɛnsere no bo a na ne bo yɛ $71.10 no mu.
Saa mfɛnsere yi bo akɔ soro paa wɔ COVID-19 amaneɛ a Delta a wagu so wɔ Europa aman bi so de abɔ kɔkɔ wɔ ɛseɛbɔ a akɔ soro wɔ United States no ho.
Bere a edi kan wɔ mfe abien mu no, Brent bo duu dɔla75 wɔ mfɛnsere no ano.
Eyi te saa titiriw bere a ɔkwan ne wimhyɛn akwantu kɔ so dɔɔso no.
Wɔkyerɛ nso sɛ ɛsiane ɛboɔ a ɛmu yɛ den wɔ Europa aman bi so, Asia ne Mediterranea Supɔw so nti, ɛnam a
Wɔhwɛ kwan sɛ, July 1st OPEC+ nhyiamu yi bɛsi gyinae wɔ adwuma a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ August mu no ho, bere a yɛkɔɔ gua so wɔ July bosome mu no.
Kyakyatoɔ ne gasoil boɔ a ɛgyina Gyinapɛn ne Poor ne Platts a ɛwɔ wiase nyinaa so no kyerɛ sɛ, saa bere no, na amanaman ntam adwadie (petrol) ne gasoil (a) ne gasoil (agal) wɔ bere no mu.
Gasoline hui sɛ boɔ yɛ den dodoɔ 3.47% sɛ wɔbɛtoto mpomma mu wɔ $694.78.78 na efi $671.45 biara mu wɔ mfɛnsere a na atwam no mu.45 biara
Kyakya bo kɔɔ soro ɔha biara mu 3.53, na ɛbɔɔ ka $597.30 fi mfɛnsere a edi kan no boɔ yɛ $576.89%.

Wɔde Nigeria South Africa abɛka aman ‘nenepa a wɔde rebɛma akwantufoɔ a wɔreba no ho. Nigeria na wɔyɛɛ saa gyinaeɛ no esiane po so hyɛn a ɛgu ne ho wɔ South Africa nti.
Mprempren wɔabara akwantufo a wɔkɔɔ South Africa wɔ nnafua 14 a atwam no sɛ wɔnnkɔ Nigeria.
Ɛsɛ sɛ Nigeria hyɛn gyinabea adwumayɛfo ne wɔn a wɔte South Africa no nya nnason atrae.
Brazil ne Turkey nso wɔ din.
Kaaka Mohammed a wokum no no yɛ awerɛhosɛm ne yawdi.
Atirimɔdensɛm a meyɛ ma abusua no ne ne kra Rest In Peace.
Nanso anyɛ yie koraa no, ebinom afi ase retwe adwene asi nsawɔsoɔ a ɛrekɔ so wɔ aban mu no so, na ebinom nso akyerɛ sɛ ɛnsɛ sɛ yɛma aban no yɛ yɛn dea.
Eyi nso nyɛ papa dodo, efisɛ ɛmma wontumi nyɛ nhwehwɛmu a ɛfata nnyɛ yiye.
“Fix The Country” rehwɛ sɛ aban no rebua asɛm yi, ɛyɛ a mennye nni sɛ ebetumi aba sɛ ɔman no bɛtwe nnipakum yi afi hɔ, ɛwom mpo sɛ minim yiye sɛ wɔ yɛn amanyɔsɛm mu no, biribiara betumi ayɛ yiye, a nea ɛka ho ne sɛ ɔbarima bi de ne ho bɛhyɛ ɔbarima ne brabɔne mu.
Aban no hyiaa akraman no sɛ wɔnsɔ wɔn nhwɛ na wɔn bo ntɔ wɔn yam.
Akyiri yi, anyɛ yiye koraa no, nsɛm ho amanneɛbɔfo baanu kyerɛkyerɛɛ nea aban reyɛ de asɛe ɔman no mu.
Nanso nokwarem no, akuturukubɔfo no bi wɔ aban no mu a ɔdaa abohuru adi denam akraman no a ɔfrɛɛ wɔn no so, na ɔsrɛɛ wɔn sɛ wɔn ankasa nni kan nhyehyɛ wɔn ho.
Afei nso, yɛwɔ yɛn Polisi Adwuma no, a mpɛn pii no ɛbɔɔ mmɔden sɛ ɛbɛhaw akraman no adwene ma wɔada no adi, sɛ wɔde Covid ho nkyerɛkyerɛmu a emu da hɔ bɛma wɔ bere a wontumi nsiw nnipadɔm a wɔwɔ Sir John ayi ase no kwan anaa wɔnhyɛ da.
Saa nneɛma yi bɔ mmɔden biara sɛ ɛbɛma ɔman no ayɛ basabasa, a nea ɛka ho ne obi a ɔyɛ katee a wokum no, a ɛyɛ mmerɛw na ntease nnim, ɛwom mpo sɛ wobetumi agye akyinnyegyefo ani esiane adanse a enni hɔ a ɛkyerɛ sɛ nsu nni hɔ nti.
Ɛsɛ sɛ yehu nso sɛ, sɛ ɛtɔ mmere bi a, yɛn amanyɔsɛm betumi ama nnipa bi a wonni aban no mu ayɛ nneɛma bɔne a ɛte saa a ɛbɛma nnipa pii ani agye aban no ho.
Ɛha nso, adanse biara nni hɔ a ɛfoa eyi so wɔ Kaaka wuo no mu.
Nanso bere a yɛresusuw tebea no ho no, ɛsɛ sɛ yɛyɛ saa wɔ akwan pii so, na yetumi kata biribiara so.
Wɔ asraafo a wonnim hwee a wɔkɔɔ so kunkum nnipa baanu no fam no, mebɔɔ wɔn sobo dodo.
Ɛsɛ sɛ yɛde mfomsoɔ a wɔayɛ ne nteteeɛ a wɔde ama wɔn no ho asodi to wɔn so.
Kɔ so ara hu amane bebree wɔ fɛreɛ a ɛmumɔn a ɛnnyɛ adwuma no mu, ɛfiri berɛ tenten a saa nnwumakuo yi de wɔn ho ahyɛ dwumadie yi mu, na ɛgyina ɛkwan a aban wɔ so sɛ ɔde manfoɔ bɛyɛ 2000 Mobrowa Struggle ne me di dwuma sɛ “Divine Drummer” no.
Yehuu sɛnea polisifo ne asraafo no ne yɛn dii nsɛm bere a na ɛsɛ sɛ wogyae yɛn wɔ honam fam mpo sɛ yɛbɛyɛ basabasa no.

Nokwarem no, ɔyɛ ɔnanani a ɔda amoa donkudonku bi mu, na ɔhyɛ asraafo atrae bi wɔtire.
Baabiara a mɛkɔ no, me ne nhomanimfoɔ ne Afrikafoɔ bi rebɛdi yɛn kaseɛbɔ ho dwuma.
Nanso wɔ sini no akyi no, wɔretwe adwene asi saa nneɛma bɔne yi so sɛ ɛne m’adwene a ɛfa Ghana ho no reko atia kwasafo
Asɛm no ne sɛ, nneɛma bi a ɛwɔ aban no mu ne mmofra no nneyɛe a ɛnam so ba bammɔ adwumayɛfoɔ a yɛne wɔn di nkitaho no yɛ ɔhaw a emu yɛ den a ɛwɔ yɛn akwantuo yi mu.
So Ghanafo a wɔyɛ ɔyɛkyerɛ de sɛe aware?
Na nsuɔhyew ne rɔba nso ɛ?
Aban betumi atow atirimɔdenfoɔ bi tuo sɛ ɔmma wɔn sɛnkyerɛnne bi a ɛbɛhyɛ wɔn ma wɔayɛ adwadifoɔ panin wɔ nnipa dodoɔ a wɔne wɔn di nsɛm ho. Aban bɛpɛ sɛ wɔma kwan ma wɔnya kwan a wɔfa so ne adwumayɛfoɔ a wɔne wɔn di nsɛm wɔ kwantenpɔn so no bɔ wɔn ho ban wɔ sukuu mu na ama wɔasan akɔbɔ wɔn adwamansɛm mu.
Eyi yɛ abufuw kɛkɛ, na ɛde biribi a ɛho nhia a wobetumi de atua bɔne so ka ba.
Ebetumi aba sɛ Ɔmanpanin de ne ho begye nsɛm mu de awerɛhyɛmu a ɛho hia ama, ɛde asomdwoe ne ɔhaw a ɛtwa toɔ
Ahobammɔ nnwumakuw no ahwere ahotoso a wɔwɔ wɔ akraman ne wɔn a wɔyɛ ɔyɛkyerɛ no anim no.
Yɛn Asomdwoe Bagua no a abɛn pɛɛ no nso ama mmarahyɛ kwan bi a ebetumi ama Bagua no de ne ho agye nsɛm mu. Ma nsɛnnennen yi ho kwan, Ɔmanpanin no ankasa de ne ho begye nsɛm mu, na ɛsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ eyi wɔ bere a
19 Thomas Amoani a wadi mfe 19 a wawie Adei Presbyterian Senior High School a Ghana Scholarshipariat de too dwa sɛ ɔkyerɛɛ Ɔmanpanin Nana Addo Dankwa Akuffo Addo aban no ho anisɔ.
Thomas Amoani a wadi mfe nwɔtwe wɔ Afrika Atɔeɛ Sukuu a Ɛto so Abien a ɛwɔ Afrika Atɔe fam no, ntɛm ara na wɔmaa no kwan sɛ onsua ade wɔ Brunel Sukuupɔn a agye din a ɛwɔ London no mu bere a ɔtwee adwene sii ahinasariat, Owura Kingsley Agyemang so no.
Abarimaa a wadi mfe 19 a ofi Asuaba a ɔbɛn Adeiso ne ahiafoɔ a waben paa no besua Economics ne Business Finance ho ade.
Obi a kan no na ɔyɛ Adeiso SHS ho sukuuni no kaa nsɛm bi de bisabisaa no nsɛm. Ɔkyerɛɛ n’asɛm no, Thomas Amoani kaa sɛnea ɔde kar twaa kilomita 12 kɔɔ sukuu no ho asɛm.
Ɔmanpanin Akufo-Addo de n’adwene sii saa asɛm yi so, na ntɛm ara ɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ
Ɔsoafoɔ a ɔtwerɛtwerɛtwerɛtwerɛtwerɛtwerɛtwerɛtwerɛtwerɛtwerɛtwerɛtwerɛtwerɛtwerɛtwerɛtwerɛtwerɛtwerɛtwerɛ firisɛ Toma a Ɔmanpanin ayɛ no bɛtwa kwan tenten bi a ɛbɛtumi akanyan afoforo ma wɔabɔ wɔn ho mmɔden wɔ wɔn nteteeɛ mu.
“Mehunu sɛ Thomases reba, na metumi ama wɔn awerɛhyem sɛ Scholarship Secretariat bɛwɔ hɔ de mmoa a ehia bɛma wɔn. Thomas asɛm no bɛkanyan afoforo a wɔte sɛ ɔno. Ɛsɛ sɛ mekamfo Ɔmanpanin Akufo-Addo wɔ ne ho a ɔde gyee nsɛm mu ntɛm so”
Arriving a ɔwɔ sukuupɔn mu, Thomas Amoani a wantumi amfa n’anigye ansie no se wayɛ krado sɛ ɔbɛma Ghana frankaa so na amma ɔman no ankɔ fam.
“Mennwen ho da sɛ Owura Ɔpanin de hokwan a ɛte saa no bɛma me wɔ Registrar adwumayɛ mu. Meda m’ase sɛ m’ahotosoɔ a ɛwɔ me mu no bɛdi me man Ghana huammɔ”
Brunel Sukuupɔn a ɛwɔ London no yɛ baguam nhwehwɛmu wɔ Uxbridge mpɔtam a ɛwɔ London, England. Wohui wɔ afe 1966 mu na wɔtoo din Victorian engineer Isambard Kingdom Brunel no, wɔyɛɛ no sɛ sukuupɔn a ɛsen biara 93 wɔ wiase nyinaa wɔ mfiridwuma ne mfiridwuma mu mpɛn 32, wɔ Europa aman mu ne 11 mu wɔ British sukuu ahorow mu.
Atɛmmuafoɔ panin Kwasi Anin Yeboah ne Mmarahyɛbɛdwafoɔ ne Member of Parliament for Bolgatan East, Dr Dominic Akuritinga Ayine at the General Legal Council (GLC).
Sɛnea mmarahyɛbɛdwani ne kan Member of Parliament for Zebilla kyerɛ no, Owura John Ndebugre, akasakasa a National Democratic Congress (NDC) ne nnipa foforo a wɔkasa tia anwiinwii no yɛ anobaabaeɛ bere a Dryine yi ne ho adi wɔ Mmarahyɛbɛdwa Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie a ɛwɔ Mmarahyɛbɛdwa
" Yesusuw sɛ ɔno ne onipa pa a ɛsɛ sɛ ɔda anwiinwii ano efisɛ asɛm a wɔka kyerɛɛ Dr Ayine no na ɛmaa saa asɛm yi bae ne sɛ, sɛ ɔde ne ho to mmaratofo no ahofadi so a, ɔkwan bi so no, wɔnam ɔkwan bi so ama ɔmampanyin no adesrɛ no ho kwan anaa wasi ne bo”
Atemmufoɔ panin no abɔ mmaranimfoɔ Dr Dominic Akuritinga Ayine a ɔda GLC ano no soboɔ sɛ ɔkaa nsɛm a ɔdii kan kaa ho asɛm wɔ Ɔmanpanin Petitions ne nkɛntɛnso a enyae wɔ Afrika Democracy so.
Wɔabɔ Dr. Ayine sobo sɛ wakasa atia Judiary ahofadi a ɛnam ɔkwan a Asennibea Kunini no faa so yii abatoɔ a ɛto so 2020 no ano.
Dr. Ayine ka sɛ n’abisadeɛ a wogyina so ka asɛm yi wɔ adesua yi mu no yɛ Asennibea Kuniniɔ no antumi amfa akwan a wɔfa so yɛ adeɛ no anyɛ adwuma, na saa ara nso na n’abisadeɛ anaa nneɛma a ɔde gyigye n’ani no nnyɛ adwuma.
Asɛnnibea Kunini no kasa tiaa Dr. Ayine sɛ wabu nsɛm a ɛte saa a wɔka tiaa Asɛnnibea Kunini no mufo wɔ Election Petition mu no ano. Dr. Ayine paa kyɛw denneennen bere a ɔkɔɔ Asɛnnibea no anim wɔ Mmarahyɛbɛdwani no anim no, na ogye toom sɛ wakasa atia Mmarahyɛbɛdwani bi a wannye ho.
Oduruyɛfo Ayine kaa wɔ ne bo a wasi sɛ ɔbɛyɛ ade atia CJ nnwiinwii no mu sɛ ne nsɛm no nsɔre ntia atemmusɛm a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ abatoɔ no so no.
Ɔkyerɛ sɛ ne nsɛm no yɛ nokware wɔ gyidi mu.
“Sɛnea maka wɔ mmuaeɛ yi mu no, sɛ́ mmaranimfoɔ no, mewɔ asɛyɛde soronko sɛ mɛkasa atia mmarahyɛbɛdwadifoɔ adwuma no. Menam me ntetee ne m’ahokokwaw so anya me ho mfaso sen me manfoɔ no mu dodow no ara.
Ɔkɔɔ so susuwii sɛ ne nsɛm no wɔ kasa a ɛfata na ɛyɛ dɛ mu.
Aban Democratic Congress (NDC) a ɛwɔ nsɛntwerɛfoɔ nhyiamu ase wɔ Nkran Dwoda no ka kyerɛɛ Mmarahyɛbɛdwani no sɛ ɔntwe n'atemmuo ano ngu Dr Ayine so.
Bere a Owura Ndebugre reka dibea a ɛsɛ sɛ Ɔtemmufo Panyin no twe n’adwene si so ho asɛm no, ɔka kyerɛɛ Dr Ayine sɛ ɛnsɛ sɛ ɔka amusiei no ho asɛm.
Ɔrekasa wɔ radio so nsɛm bi a Graphic Online a ɛwɔ Accra based Citi FM bisabisaa mu wɔ Benada anwummere (June 22, 2021) mu no, Owura Ndebugre kae sɛ: " Yegye di sɛ ɔhaw biara nni Ɔtemmufo Panyin no a ɔrekasa atia no no no
Bere a Stephen Quarcoo ne Tommy Thompson resi saa asɛm yi so dua wɔ 1996 mu - Ade a etia Mensah Bo no, ɔtow hyɛɛ ɔtemmufo bi so, enti ɔde asɛm no kɔtoo Mmarahyɛbɛdwani no anim, na afei Mmarahyɛbɛdwani no de firii mmaratoɔ no maa asɛnnibea no anaa ɔbuu atɛn.
Ɔhaw biara nni CJ ho a wɔde nwiinwii no ho
"So Misusuw sɛ ɔhaw biara nni Ɔtemmufo Panyin no ho a ɔde nwiinwii no.
Asɛm no ara ne sɛ, Dominic Ayine ne aban dwumayɛni panin panin, na ɔne n’adwumam panyin no de nkurɔfo kɔɔ asɛnnibea. Enti sɛ Aban Panyin no pene so sɛ obi bɛbu atɛn a, obi betumi aka sɛ ɔmfa ne ho nhyɛ kasa mu.
Dabi, ɛsɛ sɛ wokɔ asennibea na wofa wo asɛm no, na woka sɛ woanni fɔ wɔ soboɔ a wɔbɔɔ wo no ho.
Enti wɔ saa kwan yi ara so no, Ɔtemmufo Panyin no susuw sɛ asɛm a ɔkae no
Enti wokɔ hɔ a, saa nsɛm yi nyinaa a NDC ne Dr Ayine nkekaeɛ no ara regye ho akyinnyeɛ no yɛ nsɛm a ɛsɛ sɛ ɛkɔ so wɔ asuafoɔ Ndebugrekuo mu" Owura Ndebugre de kaa ho.
Bere a ɔrekyerɛkyerɛ mu sɛ ɔmpɛ sɛ ɔbɛka mfaso a ɛwɔ so ho asɛm no, ɔkyerɛe sɛ akwan abien na ɛwɔ hɔ a wɔfa so bu no animtiaa, bere a asɛm no da so ara wɔ hɔ, na sɛ woka atemmusɛm no kyerɛ wo a, ɛno na ɛbɛma woabu w’ani agu atemmuo so, na
Sɛ wo werɛ fi asɛm bi wɔ asɛnnibea a, wubetumi aka sɛ wo ne no nyɛ adwene, " bu no saa. Mereka sɛ mempɛ sɛ me ne no besusuw mfaso a ɛwɔ so no ho, afei na nea mereyɛ ara ne sɛ me ne no nyɛ adwene wɔ dibea a esiane amanyɔkuw no nti, ɔno [Dr Ayine kyerɛɛ hokwan a ɔwɔ sɛ ɔka asɛm no ho. Enti ɛnsɛ sɛ me
" Asɛntitiriw no ne sɛ wobɛkɔ Ntemmuafoɔ Nkabomkuo no nkyɛn na woaka sɛ wowɔ hokwan sɛ wuyi asɛm no fi mu, nanso wuntumi nka sɛ Ɔtemmuafoɔ no ntumi nnwiinwii, ɔno ara ne n’awerɛhyɛmuɔ no ti, na woka sɛ w’ahotosoɔ no mu ahotosoɔ a wowɔ wɔ kwaa no mu no yɛ den.
Yebisaa Ayine sɛ, Ɔtemmuafoɔ panin yi gyina GLC ano, ma enti asuafoɔ no yɛ n’atosoɔ boafoɔ, enti ɔresoma Ayine akɔ n’ankasa "court " sɛ wɔnsɔ ano, Owura Ndebugre na wabua wo sɛ, “Ateeɛ a yɛfrɛ wɔn a yɛfrɛ wɔn “Ntemmua”
Ɔde Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie Soafoɔ a watwe nkurɔfo aso wɔ hɔ no dii dwuma, na ɔkaa sɛ, “haahaa saa nkurɔfo no adwene anaa wɔn kasa kwa. Sɛ mokɔ na moka sɛ wɔn nyinaa aporɔw a adanse biara nni ho a, wɔbɛtwe mo akɔ Privilege Boayikuw no mu. Adɛn nti na
" Nka sɛ Ɔtemmufo Panyin no teɛ anaa ɛnteɛ.
Nea mereka ara ne sɛ Ɔtemmuafoɔ panin no de asɛm no akɔto dwa sɛ wabu mmara so, na ɔno ara na ɔdi atɛmmuo no anim na wakasa atia no.
Anwiinwii no nkyerɛ sɛ wɔabu wo fɔ, na ɛsɛ sɛ wokɔ hɔ, na wofa nsɛntwerɛfoɔ nhyiamu ne nea ɛkeka ho nyinaa, na ɛno ansa na asɛm no besi.
Ɛyɛ bere a wobɛkɔ hɔ na adanse wɔ hɔ a ɛkyerɛ sɛ wowɔ hɔ, na wubetumi afi ase anwiinwii, nanso misusuw sɛ, saa bere yi de, me ne Ayine retu Ayine fo sɛ ɔmmɔ mmɔden na ɔnkɔ Ntemmuofoɔ no nkyɛn na ɔmfa n’asɛm no nkɔ, ɛyɛ wɔn anigye sɛ wɔbɛkɔ
Ɔman Asomdwoe Bagua (NPC) no afi ase ayɛ nhyehyɛe a ɛbɛma ɔman no ayɛ biako denam man no asomdwoe a ɛbɛbɔ ɔman no ho ban wɔ afe a etwaam no abatoɔ akyi no so.
Sɛnea bagua no kyerɛ no, amanyɔsɛm mu akuturukubɔ yɛ ɔsɛmpɔw titiriw a na ebetumi de ɔhaw bi aba, enti ɛho hia sɛ wɔhyɛ no bɔs mu.
NPC kaa saa asɛm yi kyerɛɛ amanyɔkuo ne akuo ahodoɔ a ɛwɔ Ada a ɛwɔ Nuklea Akɛseɛ Mantam mu.
Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie no ne Amanaman Nkabom Mpɔntu Adwumayɛ Adwumayɛfoɔ (UNDP) no gyinaa adwadie ne
Na botae no ne sɛ wɔbɛsi akan akan wɔ akuturukubɔ mu de ahyɛ aman nkabom, amanyɔsɛm mu mpaapaemu, asomdwoe ne ɔman nkabom a ɛnam so no mu den.

Owura Dery kaa sɛ ɛmfa ho sɛ wɔgyinaa banbɔ nhyehyɛe a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ December aban abadiakyire no anim no, wɔkɔɔ so ara kaa basabasayɛ bi a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ hɔ, na ɛmaa ebinom hweree wɔn nkwa, na ɛde wɔn kɔɔ agyapade mu.
Ɔkaa sɛ apolisifoɔ a wɔwɔ ɔman no mu nnum na wɔyɛɛ atirimmɔdensɛm 32 ho kyerɛwtohɔ, na nnipa baasia wuwuiɛ.

Owura Kan - Hapaah ka kyerɛɛ amanyɔsɛm mu akontabuo ne adwadifoɔ sɛ wɔn nnyɛ den mma ɔman no sikasɛm ne amanyɔsɛm mu nkɔsoɔ.
Rt Hon. Scotland no kamfoo Ghana manfoɔ wɔ asomdwoeɛ a wɔgyee amanyɔsɛm ho ɔkasaɛ wɔ ɔman no mu no ho.
Sɛnea Ghana kyerɛ no, abakɔsɛm kyerɛ no, na ɔde dodow amammu adi dwuma, na ɔkae sɛ " ɛyɛ adesoa duruduru ma nkurɔfo no, nanso ɛyɛ adesoa a ɔman no de hoahoa wɔn ho daa wɔ Ghana.
Nanso, ɔsrɛe sɛ wɔmma mmea bebree ne mmeranteɛ ne mmabaa ntena ɔman no mu.
Mmarahyɛbɛdwani a ɔda NPC ano, Adi. Dr Ernest Adu-Gyamfi, kaa sɛ n’adwuma ne sɛ ɔde ne nsa bɛhyɛ abɛɛfo adwadie mu den na ɔde ne ho ato aban abadiakyire so.
Ɔkyerɛɛ anidaso a ɛwɔ hɔ sɛ nsɛmpɔw a yɛasusuw ho yi betumi de apirakuru a wɔyɛɛ no afe 2020 abatoɔ akyi no aba.
Asoeɛ panin a ɔda Transeco Minerals ne Mining ano, Owura Godwin Amarh ayɛ sukuu dan a ɛtoa so nsia wɔ Apatia Mantam mu wɔ Atiwa West Mantam mu.
Wobuu akontaa sɛ, adesuadan no boɔ yɛ GH295,000, a ɛyɛ adwumakuo no fã a wɔfrɛ no Corporate Social Resentent (CSR).
Bere a Owura Amarh rekasa wɔ ahodwira mu no, osii so dua sɛ ɛho hia sɛ wɔma mmofra nhomasua papa ne ntetee pa bere a ɛboa ma wonya nhyɛase pa wɔ nhomasua mu no.
Ɔkaa sɛ, sɛ ɔman biara bɛtumi anya nhomasua ho nteteeɛ wɔ adesua mu a, ɛnnyɛ yie. Ɛno nti na ɔne n’adwuma
“Yei a ɛwɔ Transeco Mining ne Minerals Company no asi gyinae sɛ ɛbɛma mmofra a wɔwɔ nkurow a yɛkyerɛkyerɛ wɔn adesua ne nneɛma a atwa yɛn ho ahyia mu no ani aku nhomasua ne ntetee ho. Ɛno nti na yɛde nhomasua asɛn yɛn adwuma so no.
M'ani gye sɛ mɛsan de dwumadie yi ahyɛ sukuu yi nsa. Yɛn nyinaa nim sɛnea nhomasua ho hia ma ankorankoro ne ɔman no. Sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wobenya sukuufo a wɔn nhomasua kɔ anim kɛse no, ɛsɛ sɛ wodi kan nya nhyɛase a emu yɛ den a ɛno nti na yɛasi saa Abibirekyi yi.
Owura Amarh kaa sɛ sukuu no yɛ asɛnhia ma mpaninfoɔ ne nnipa a wɔkura ayɔnkofa pa mu fi berɛ a wɔfii wɔn dwumadie ase wɔ mpɔtam hɔ no.
Owura Amarh de n’abufuo ne nsusuiɛ bɔne a aban no de ato fagudeɛtubea nnwuma so wɔ ɔman no mu, na ɔkaa ho asɛm sɛ ɛnyɛ ne kwan so, na mmom ɛyɛ atoro.
Sɛnea ɔkyerɛ no, aban de nhyehyɛeɛ foforo, nhyehyɛeɛ ne dwumadie ahorow asi nketekrakye sɛ wɔbɛyɛ fagudeɛtubea nnwuma nketenkete na ɛnyɛ nea ɛsɛe ade.
“Marara dwumadie sɛ fagudeɛtufoɔ nnyɛ adwuma, na mmom fagudeɛyɛfoɔ ne kwaeɛ a atwa mu ahyia sɛ adaneɛ a wɔnni fahodie biara. Enti nea aban reka ne sɛ, ɛsɛ sɛ wɔn a wɔtu fagudeɛ no
Enti ɔhyɛɛ wɔn a wotu fagudeɛ no nkuran sɛ wɔnkɔyɛ adwuma nanso ɔnhwɛ mma wɔnnyɛ adwuma wɔ mmeae a wɔyɛɛ saa nneɛma no.
Owura Amarh a ɔno nso bu bɔ ho sɛ Ghana Ɔman no Small Small Scale Miners (GNASM) no tu kuw no mufo fo sɛ wɔmmoa wɔn wɔ mmeae a wɔwɔ awerɛkyekye no.
Ɔkaa sɛ fagudeɛtufoɔ nyɛ adwuma nsesaeɛ no sɛ wɔn a wɔtu fagudeɛ no firi amanfoɔ so na wɔntua hwee.
Ɔkaa sɛ, nkontia nketenkete pii reyɛ saa dedaw, nanso bebree wɔ hɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ.
“Yɛyɛ adwuma wɔ mmeae a yɛyɛ adwuma wɔ hɔ no. Enti ɛsɛ sɛ yɛyere yɛn ho tu anammɔn. Minim paa sɛ yɛn asafo no mufo ne afoforo pii a wɔasisi sukuu no boa ma anyinam ahoɔden ba ɔman no mu. Ɛsɛ sɛ yepia saa nsɛm no ma nkurɔfo a wɔwɔ hɔ no sesa wɔn sikasɛm mu nhwehwɛmu a ɛkyerɛ sɛ nkontimmaa no sɛe kɛkɛ no.
Rebecca Foundation no ne Abdul Samad Rabiu Africa Initiative (ASR Africa) ayɛ Memorandum of Understanding (MoU) ho sɛnkyerɛnne.
Wɔbɛyi sika yi afi ASR Africa dɔla ɔpepem 00 wɔ Afrika Social Development ne Renewal de aboa Rebecca Foundation nhomasua no.
Ɔrekasa wɔ nhyiamu yi ase no, Managing Director a ɔda ASR Africa ano, Owura Ubon Udoh, kamfoo fapem a ɛmaa mmea ne mmofra a wɔwɔ ɔman no mu nyaa ahofama maa wɔn yiyedi.
Ɔkamfoo nhyɛaseɛ a ɛgyinaa so maa adwumakuo pa a ɛboa ma fagudeɛ ne nnwuma a ɛboa ma wɔnya kwan yie wɔ sukuukɔ ne apɔmuden ne mmaa sikasɛm mu adwadie mu.
"We yɛɛ yɛn sukuu dwumadie yi na ɔkyerɛɛ Rebecca Foundation no sɛ ɛyɛ adɔekuo a wɔagye din paa wɔ Ghana a ɛhyɛɛ ASR Africa nkuran sɛ ɔmmoa Rebecca Foundation”
Abenfo panin a ɔda Dwumadie no ano, Owurayere Rebecca Akuffo-Addo de aseda ama ASR Africa sɛ ɔmmoa nhyɛase no.
Ɔhyɛɛ fapem no bɔ sɛ ɔde bɛbue ama adwadie no so mfasoɔ ama mmofra ntetee wɔ ɔman no mu.
UK de ne ho ahyɛ Nnamdi Kanu, a ɔyɛ kuw bi a wɔabara wɔn sɛ wɔnkɔhwehwɛ baabi a wɔbɛtena wɔ Nigeria anafo fam apuei, baabi a nnipa a wofi Igbo no dɔɔso no mu.
“Saa, Owura Kanu, a ɔwɔ Britain ne Nigeria mantam mu no, Interpol mmoa so na ɔde no kɔɔ Nigeria, sɛnea mmaranimfo panyin no kyerɛ no.
Ohyiaa sobo a wɔde bɔɔ no wɔ Nigeria no, nanso oguan fii ɔman no mu afe 2017 bere a na ɔda abrannaa so no.
Yɛaka no pen sɛ ebia wɔkyeree no wɔ UK, baabi a wogye di sɛ ɔno titiriw na ogyina hɔ no.
“Yebetumi asi so dua sɛ wɔankyere Nnamdi Kanu wɔ UK sɛ wadi n’atirimɔdensɛm bi nti, British High Commission kasamafoɔ no ka kyerɛɛ BBC.
Mprempren ɔwɔ Nigeria sum ase polisifoɔ berɛ a asɛnnibea ketewaa bi aba Benada no.
Wɔhwɛ kwan sɛ obedi n'asɛm no bio wɔ July 26 mu.
Ɔbaa a wadi mfe 53 no begyee din wɔ afe 2009 mu bere a ofii ase Radio Biafra ne akasam fii London kɔɔ Nigeria.
Mfe anum akyi no, ɔhuu nnipa a wɔwɔ Biafra (Ipob) a Nigeria atumfoɔ no de ato dwa sɛ amumɔyɛfo bi ahyɛ wɔn nsa.

M'ani gyei bere a mihui sɛ wɔresiesie Square no awie afe a etwaam no.
Wɔyɛɛ aduru yi a wɔde ka dan ho ne nnwuma a wɔyɛ de siesiee Square no maa kan Ɔmanpanin Jerry John Rawlings ayi no.
Asuae a ɛwɔ Abɔmmɔfoɔ-Ghana (IoD - Gh) akamfo Ghana Sikakorabea (BoG) sɛ watu anammɔn atitiriw bi a ɛbɛma ɔman no sodi atu mpɔn.
Abɛdwakuo a ɛwɔ akoraeɛ ne akoraeɛ no ntam sɛ wɔbɛtumi aboa ama nnwumakuo ahodoɔ a ɛwɔ ɔman yi mu no anya nkɔsoɔ.
Ɔsoafoɔ a ɔda BoG ano, IoD-Gh panin, Owura Rockson Kwesi Dogbeah de too dwa sɛ, Dr Ernest Addison ama wasesa ne kannifo wɔ sikasɛm mu nsakrae mu.
Ɔkaa sɛ, adwuma a Dr Addison yɛeɛ no ama sikakorabea dwumayɛni bi a ɔwɔ sika foforɔ aba so.
Asɛm bi a adesuabea no de too dwa ne sɛ wɔbɛkamfo sikakorabea no wɔ dwuma titiriw a ɛredi wɔ adwuma pa a ɛwɔ Ghana man mu no ho, na wɔrehwehwɛ abusuabɔ pa a ɛda BoG ne nsiakyibaa ntam no.
Bere a Owura Dogbeah rekasa wɔ IoD-Gh dwumadie yi ho no, ɔkaa sɛ IoD-Gh no reyɛ adwadifoɔ a ɔresi akan wɔ abrabɔ gyinapɛn a ɔde bɛyɛ adwuma wɔ Ghana.
Ɔdaa no adi sɛ ɔman mmara mu nkɔso yɛ dwumadi titiriw foforo a adesuabea no de asi hɔ.
Ɔka kyerɛɛ wɔn sɛ adesuabea yi de mfasoɔ a ɛwɔ so sɛ ɛbɛbɔ mmɔden ahyɛ nneɛma a nnipa a wɔda nsow ne nnwumakuo ahodoɔ a ɛgyina hɔ ma akakabensɛmdie ne nnwumakuo ahodoɔ a ɛgyina hɔ ma adwumakuo ahodoɔ a wɔdi manfoɔ anim ne nnwumakuo ahodoɔ no ho no ama Ghana sikasɛm ntotoe.
Ɔtoaa so sɛ, adesuabea yi ne wɔn a wɔyɛ adwuma wɔ abɛɛfo nsawɔsoɔ abɔ Ghana Integrated Thinking ne Reporting dwumadie a wɔyɛɛ no adwadie mu no ahyɛ akwannya ne adwadie a wɔnam abɛɛfo adwadie ne adwadie so anya mfasoɔ wɔ adwadie ne adwadie mu.
BoG Amrado kaa sɛ adwumakuo yi di dwuma titiriw wɔ sikasɛm mu.
Sɛdeɛ ɔkyerɛ no, adwumakuo no kyerɛ sɛ, nnwumayɛbea sohwɛbea adwumayɛfoɔ ne wɔn a wɔyɛ adwuma wɔ nnwumakuo no mu no, ɛnam nneɛma a ɛde sikasɛm mu nkorabata ahodoɔ bi abatoɔ ne wɔn adwadie abadiakyire
Osii so dua sɛ ɛhia sɛ Ghana manfoɔ bɛtumi agyina adwadie nnwuma pa ano, na ɔde sika a sikakorabea no de boa adwuma a ɛwɔ sikakorabea hɔ no ahyɛ wɔn nsa, ɛnkanka berɛ a nsɛm a ɛrekɔ so wɔ sikakorabea hɔ no anya Ghana sikasɛm mu fekusɛm so nkɛntɛnsoɔ.
Ɛsɛ sɛ Arteta gye bere foforo
Sɛnea madi kan aka no, Arsenal nyɛɛ n'adwene sɛ ɔbɛtwe Mikel Arteta ne n'adwadifoɔ no asan de no akɔ Gunners wɔ bere a edi hɔ no mu.
Obiara ntumi nka mma ebinom sɛ Arsenal asi gyinae pa nanso bɔɔlbɔ kuw no ayɛ wɔn adwene sɛ wɔde wɔn ho bɛhyɛ agumadifo a wɔwɔ ɔdom akyɛde pii mu wɔ ahohuru bere yi mu.
Wɔrebisa nsɛm a ɛyɛ hu afa adwuma so panyin no ho, na wɔ n’ahosiesie mu mpo no, wɔn a wɔhwɛ ne ho no rehwɛ no, na wɔresusuw ho sɛ ɔno ne onipa a ɔfata ma adwuma no anaa.
Arteta a wadi mfe 39 agye din wɔ Pep Guardiola nkyɛn sɛ obi a ɔka ne ho.
Nanso, bosome dunson akyi no, Arsenal aban no nnyaa nkɔsoɔ, na nnipa bebree rennye ntom sɛ dwumadie no nyɛ papa sɛ wɔn a wɔwɔ Unai Emery, ɔbarima a osii n'ananmu bɔɔ no fii Europa Apam no mu.
Arteta hyɛɛ Arsenal nsa, na nkratasin no maa wɔn akwaaba sɛ wɔn kɛtɛ, nanso bere a wɔrehwɛ Chelsea ne Tottenham no, wɔn ho retɔ wɔn.
Ɔhaw a Ɛkyɛn So no werɛ remfi da
Nanso metumi aka akyerɛ wo sɛ Kroenke wuranom no nni baabiara
Sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a Arteta bɛsi akan ama atwene, ahyehyɛ kuw a ɛyɛ den na wafa akwan a ɔfa so no so wɔ bere a ɛfata mu no, Gunners betumi abɔ ho ban na wɔahyew no.
De Gea gye tom sɛ No2
Ɛmfa ho sɛ Manchester a ɔyɛ adwuma wɔ sotɔɔ mu no, David De Gea nyaa nhyehyɛeɛ bi kosii sɛ n’adwumayɛfo 2023 rehwɛ nsuo no mu ahwɛ baabi a n'ani bɛgye ho sɛ ɔde ne nsa bɛhyɛ ase.
Mewɔ Old Trafford mu sɛ ɛmfa ho sɛ me ne No1 Dean Henderson wɔ nkitahodi pa no, De Gea rentra benkyi no so nkyɛ.
Merefa anigye afi Atletico Madrid, Paris Saint Germain ne Madrid.
Ɛwom sɛ abofra a wadi mfe 30 no bi a ɔwɔ kuw no mu gye di sɛ wagyae adwuma kakra wɔ mfe abien a atwam no mu de, nanso n’adwuma no so bɛtew koraa.
Manager Solskjaer kaa sɛ, “Goal officeer no yɛ kuw a wɔn ho yɛ den paa.
Wɔyɛ adwuma de siesie wɔn ho, ɛsono sɛnea wɔn mu biara yɛ n’ade, wɔn mu biara yɛ ne dea, na wɔbom yɛ nneɛma pii.
Akyinnye biara nni ho sɛ, wɔn nsa aka abusuabɔ ne honhom a ɛwɔ botae yi ho dwumadie mu.
Ɛyɛ akansi a ɛfata.
Mewɔ awerɛhyem sɛ nea ɔka ne ho no yɛ nokware, sɛ Gea san gye No1 a ɔhyɛ n'atade mu no tom na ɔde ne nsa to benkyi no so wɔ agodi a ɛho hia mu a, ɛyɛ me nwonwa sɛ ɔbɛpam me afi Old Trafford.
Mefa West Brom san kogye m'ahome bio
Bere bi akyi wɔ Premier League mu no, yɛsan kaa asɛmpa no kyerɛɛ West Bromwich Albion.
Ade titiriw a ɛbɛma wɔasan agye wɔn a wɔtwentwɛn wɔn nan ase wɔ Apɔnkɔ so ne sɛ, ebetumi aba sɛ Sam Allardyce a ɔyɛ odumgya adwuma no kwankyerɛfo abadiakyire no bɛpene so ma watra mu.
N'aba mu abu sɛ wahwere din pa a wahwere sɛ wɔde bɔɔlbɔ kuw bi ne nneduafo a wɔwɔ Brom Atɔe fam no anya adwuma pii ayɛ bere a wɔpɛ sɛ wɔkora ne so no.
Ainsley Maitland-Niles, Conor Gallagher ne Okay Yokuslu bɛsan akɔ wɔn awofo nkyɛn wɔ boseabɔ mu nanso Matheus Pereira, Callum Robinson, Hal Robson-Ka ne Karlan Grant betumi ama wɔn ani agye saa asɛm yi ho.
Ɔbarima a Ɔsen Biara Wɔ Kurow Mu
Hena ne obi a odi akoten paa wɔ Manchester City squad mu?
Dabi, ɛyɛ Raheem Sterling.
Manager Pep Guardiola yɛɛ adeyɛ bi a na ɛsɛ sɛ agumadini biara yɛ de hwɛ bɔɔl ne n'afa a ɛto so du.
Atukɔfo bi wɔ Kurow no mu a wɔn ho yɛ hare nanso Gabriel Yesu daa ne ho adi sɛ ɔno ne obi a odi mmuada.
Ade a eye sen biara ne sɛ yebefi Havertz
Thomas Tuchel ato Kai Havertz ayeyi nnwom na watwe adwene asi botae abien a ɔde asisi Fulham anim nnansa yi no so.
Tuchel ka sɛ efi bere a Kai duu Stamford Bridge a efi Bayer Leverkusen bae no, nneɛma nkɔ yiye wɔ German kasa mu.
Akwantu a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ ɔman foforo so a na ɛsɛ sɛ wɔdi mmara so no maa nneɛma mu kɔɔ so yɛɛ den maa Covid-19, na na ɛsɛ sɛ wɔko tia sɛ wɔbɛyɛ pɛ.
Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie a ɛtwa toɔ no ne nea ɛdi hɔ a yɛfrɛ no Tuchel nso gye di sɛ ɔbɛdi dwuma yie wɔ akonta a ɛtwa toɔ no mu.
Solskjaer redan Unitedfo bio
Ebetumi aba sɛ Manchester United ne wɔn a wɔtɔn atuo no redi apere denneennen sɛ wɔbɛko atia wɔn wuranom nanso gyidi foforo bi wɔ kuw no mu a ɛbɛma wɔanya ahotoso foforo sɛ wobetumi anya nkɔso.
Ɔbarima a n'ani da ne so ne Olenner Solskjaer, na ɔne United adwumayɛfo ne n'akyitaafo pii kasae dapɛn yi no, obiara gye tom sɛ bere aso sɛ oyi adwuma sohwɛfo no ayɛ wɔ asram dunwɔtwe a atwam no mu.
Solskjaer bɔɔ kwan maa ɔde ne nsa hyɛɛ Bruno Fernandes ne Edinson Cavani ase, na n'abien nyinaa ayɛ nea wotumi yɛ wɔ United States santen mu.
Cavani asi so dua sɛ ɔreyɛ adwuma foforo, na ɛno ne gyidi a ɔwɔ wɔ Solskjaer a wadaadaa no.
Paul Pogba buu n’ani guu so, na ɔne n’adwumam panyin no ntam yɛɛ kama.
Sɛ United di nkonim wɔ akansi mu nnansa yi a, wɔsan sɔre, ko ntɔkwaw mpɛn pii sen sɛ wobedi nkonim.
Ade baako wɔ hɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ yɛda Adwadifoɔ panin, Vice-Chairman Ed Woodward ase, na ɛnam so ma Solskjaer bere di yiye wɔ adwuma no mu.
Mprempren, Solskjaer ne adwuma a ɛho hia sen biara ne fapem a ɛyɛ den sen biara a ɛwɔ United ne akasatiafo ne adwumayɛfoɔ ne wɔn a wogye di sɛ eyi ne bere a sika kɔkɔɔ wɔ hɔ ma Reds no mfiase.
Nsɛnkyerɛnne
Kane dwen ho sɛ obefi hɔ akɔ
Mihuu kommyɛ titiriw bi wɔ dapɛn no awiei wɔ Leeds akansi no mu.
Harry Kane ntaa ntu mmirika mmoro so, na mmom obiara a ɔdi agoru no, sɛ ɔnni bi na ɔhyɛ mmara ne akwankyerɛ a ɔde bɛma akuturukubɔfo foforɔ wɔ ɔkwan a etu mpɔn so.
Wɔ Leeds fam no, na ɔyɛ dinn na na ɔkorɔn sen sɛnea misusuw sɛ mahu no pɛn.
Misusuw sɛ eyi yɛ sɛnkyerɛnne a ɛkyerɛ sɛ Harry adwenem yɛ no nãã wɔ du a ohu wɔ Spurs no ho, na ɔrehwehwɛ ɔkwan a ɔbɛfa so afi mu.
Akuturuku rehwehwɛ obi a wapira
Mprempren Nuno Espirito Santos agye atom sɛ wɔ po so hyɛn no mpomma mu no, ɛsɛ sɛ odi kan de ne nsa hyɛ krataa foforo ase.
Nkuraa Pedro Neto ne mfinimfini wɔ Ruben Neves ne wɔn a wodi anim a ɛkyerɛ mmerɛwyɛ a ɛwɔ Wolves no.
Fabio Silva ne Raul Jimenez di kan twerɛ nsɛm yi, ɛmfa ho sɛ Jimenez akeka ne ho fi November mu bere a ɔkyɛɛ ne tikora mu no.
Wolves nni botae 13 wɔ saa bere yi mu sen afe a etwaam no.
Wolves no ahyɛ Nuno sika bɔ sɛ ɔde ne nsa bɛhyɛ ne botae ase.
Jimenez a ɛnam kwan so no bɛdi mfeɛ dummiɛnsa wɔ Kɔtɔnima da a ɛtɔ so dumiɛnsa.
Watete no asram abien nanso wɔabara no sɛ ɔmmra bɔɔl no anim na ɔne ne mfɛfo no mmɔ.
Sir Alex yi McTominay ayɛ
Bere a Sir Alex Ferguson ka Manchester United ho asɛm no, ɛfata sɛ yetie no bere nyinaa.
Adwadie a ɔde maa Scott McTominay no yɛ kɛse, na owura no ka sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ nkontabuo di agoru wɔ United agodie biara mu.
Sir Alex kae sɛ, “Scott McTominay yi ne ho adi sɛ United bɔɔlbɔfo akɛse no mu baako.
“Wohwɛ kwan sɛ United bɛpaw wɔn kuw no ma wɔadi agoru bi a ɛho hia, McTominay din wɔ mu.
Ɔyɛ onipa pa ne obi a ɔtete afoforo yiye.

Wɔrehyɛ hygienic hygienic hygiene dwumadie no ho nkuran mmom sen sɛ wɔbɛtwɛn ama obi a wosusuw sɛ wanya wɔn no de wɔn akɔ ayaresabea.
Caps United pani Lewis Uri panin ka sɛ wɔatumi asiesie wɔn haw wɔ wɔn bɔɔlbɔ kuw no ho, na abɔmmɔfo no afi ase resiesie wɔn ho ama Castle Premier Socer League akansie.
Bere a Uri rekasa akyerɛ Studio 7 no, ɔkae sɛ wɔmaa agodifo no sika soronko.
Nanso ɔkaa sɛ bosome a etwaam no, wɔbɛtua wɔn a wɔtɔ nnɔmmarima no ka. Ɔbɔɔ amanneɛ nso sɛ nnipa bi wɔ hɔ a wɔato wɔn din wɔ Caps United bɔɔlbɔ mu.
Uri kae sɛ ɔkaa asɛm no kyerɛɛ agodifo no, na ɔkaa nea enti a wɔtwentwɛn wɔn nan ase sɛ wobetua agodifo no ne sɛ na ɛyɛ den ma obiara a ɔwɔ ɔman no mu na aban ankasa no antua sika afe a etwaam no.
Nna mu hokwan ho animdefo ka sɛ ɛho hia sɛ wɔhyɛ mmara a etia nyinsɛn a wotu gu ho de bɔ mmeawa ne mmea nkwa ho ban.
Kaendisa Ndlovu of SayWhat ka sɛ ɔmanfoɔ nnim mmara a ɛtu nyinsɛn gu no, na wɔka sɛ ɛhia sɛ aban bɔ mmara no so.
Ndlovu ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ ɛho hia sɛ wɔsesa mmara no mu sɛnea na wɔakyerɛw no bere tenten ni. Ɔkae sɛ mmara ho hia na ama wɔatumi de nneɛma foforo a ebetumi ama wɔapɔn yafunu aka ho.
Ndlovu kaa nneɛma bi te sɛ adwenemyareɛ, HIV / AIDS, anaa dɛmdi ho asɛm. Nneɛma bi wɔ hɔ a yɛbɛtumi ayɛ de ayi nyinsɛn agu.
Ndlovu san kyerɛkyerɛɛ mu sɛ mmara a ɛwɔ hɔ yi nkyerɛ sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ aban ayaresabea ahorow yi nyinsɛn gu, na ɛnhwehwɛ sɛ ɔyarehwɛfo anaa oduruyɛfo bɛsa obi wɔ mmara kwan so.
Ms . Tendaishe Changamire, ɔman bahodini a ɔwɔ hokwan sɛ ɔdi mmara so wɔ nkrahyɛbɛdwafie mu no ahyɛ mmara sɛ
Ms . Changamire ka sɛ nhwehwɛmu pii kyerɛ sɛ mmaayewa nkumaa nam nyinsɛn a wotu gu so rehwere wɔn nkwa.
Ɛwom sɛ mmerante ne mmabaa pii repiapia mmara sɛ wɔnsakra mmara no de, nanso mmea mpanyimfo binom sɔre tia saa mmara no, sɛ wɔka sɛ, ɛnsɛ sɛ wɔma nyinsɛn a wotu gu no gye tom kɛse, na wɔka sɛ ɛbɛma mmerante ne mmabaa ani nnye abrabɔ ho.
Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie bi hyɛɛ Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu kena wɔ afe 1977 mu ansa na ɔman no anya fahodie.
Polisifo akyere MDC-T a Nelson Chamisa di wɔn anim no bebree bere a wɔbɔɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛkɔ adwumayɛbea ti a ɛwɔ Morgan Tsvangirai House no.
Eyi bae bere a MDC mu nokware a Ms Thokozani Khupe di anim no kyeree me no.
Asɛnnibea Kunini no abɔ Ms Khupe soboɔ sɛ ɔgyina Morgan Tsvangirai wuo akyi mfe mmienu ni.
Polisifo a ɔda afiase no bi ne Chamisa akuo mmienu, Tendai Biti ne Lynett Karenyi Kore, ne David Chimi, Lovemore Chinosa ne Gladys Hlatywayo ne afoforo.
Wɔkae sɛ apolisifoɔ no nam kwan so rekɔ adwumayɛbea ti hɔ, baabi a polisifo atwa wɔn ho ahyia no.
Studio7 ntumi ntee nnipa dodow a wɔakyere wɔn no ho asɛm mfii polisifo hɔ, na wate sobo a wɔde abɔ wɔn sɛ polisini Paul Nyathi kasamafo.
Chamisa MDC kasamafo, Fadzai Mahere kaa sɛ akyere no no maa ne ho dwiriw no.
MDC tebea no yɛ du a wɔredi Asɛnnibea Kunini bi asɛm wɔ afe yi mu a wɔhyɛɛ sɛ Chamisa ne Ms Khupe n'ananmusifoɔ no nyɛ amanyɔ mmara, na saa berɛ no na ɛsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ Congress wɔ berɛ a Ms Khupe yɛ adwuma wɔ adwuma mu.
Yei akyi no, Ms Khupe gyaa mmarahyɛbɛdwakuo no mufo baanan, na ɔka kyerɛɛ wɔn sɛ nkurɔfoɔ no nnnyina wɔn amanyɔkuo no anim bio.
Asiane ne Thabitha Khumalo, Prosper Mutseyami, Lilian Timveous ne Charlton Hwende.
Zimbabwefoɔ bi ka sɛ wɔhyɛɛ wɔn sɛ wontu mfi ɔman no mu ɛsiane Robert Mugabe mmara a ɔde akuma redi so nti.
Amammuisɛm ho nimdefo bi a ɔkyerɛ ade wɔ Bergen Sukuupɔn mu wɔ Norway, ne Zimbabwe Yibuya / Mayibuye Zimbabwe ahyehyɛde mu, Dr Victor Chimhutu ka sɛ, ɛwom sɛ wohui sɛ Owura Mugabe yɛ Afrikani baako abusua de, nanso Zimbabwean ammu no saa.
Dr Chimhutu ka sɛ Owura Mugabe ne Afrika akannifo foforo ayɛ apam, na ɛno ne ade biako nti a wanya obu kɛse afi Afrika akannifo hɔ.
Wɔbɛkae Owura Mugabe nso sɛ ɔkaa n'adwenkyerɛ kyerɛɛ Atɔeɛ ne kasatia a ɔde baa aman bi te sɛ United States ne Britain so no.
Yei kyerɛ sɛ Owura Mugabe ammɔ akraman no na ɔde no siei sɛ ne Zanu PF kuw no mufo atɔ sin anaa wɔadidi wɔn a wɔsɔre tia wɔn no atɛm mpo a.
Wɔhwɛ kwan sɛ wɔbɛto Owura Mugabe ahome Kwasida, ɛwom sɛ wɔmmɔɔ n'afasu no ho amanneɛ de.
Nnuruyɛfo ne ayarehwɛfo a wɔyɛ adwuma wɔ ɔmanfo ayaresabea no aka akyerɛ aban sɛ sɛ wontua wɔn ka ansa na December awiei aba a, wobegyae adwuma no.
Zimbabwe Ayaresabea Fekuw no titrani, Fortune Nyamande, a ɔkaa sɛ n’ahyehyɛde no yɛ Zimbabwe Nurses Association no dɛ sɛ wakyerɛw krataa akɔma aban no sɛ ɔmma wɔn kwan.
Dr Nyamande kae sɛ wakyerɛw krataa akɔma aban no sɛ ɔmmɔ ne tuo no mfidie da a ɛtɔ so du
Wɔka sɛ wɔne ayarehwɛfo a wɔwɔ aban ayaresabea no ayɛ nhyehyɛe yi anamɔn boɔ a wɔntuaeɛ da a wɔn nsa nkaa wɔn sika bosome biara ne sika a aban no de ahyɛ wɔn bɔ no so.
Dr Nyamande kasa tiaa aban no sɛ ɔmfa nsɛm ho amanneɛbɔfo nyɛ atesɛm nkrataa basabasa.
Ɔsoafoɔ panin Patrick Chinamasa adi kan abɔ amanneɛ sɛ aban ntumi ntua n’adwumayɛfo bi ka wɔ afe yi mu esiane sika a wonni nti.
"Mr Chinamasa nam atesɛm nkrataa so aka nsakraeɛ a ɛrekɔ so wɔ yɛn kaseɛbɔ mu no ho asɛm, enti yɛde akwan koro no ara na ɛbɛdi dwuma." Dr Nyamande kaa sɛ.
Wɔaka akyerɛbɔfo a wɔnyaa wɔn akatua Dwoda no ho asɛm wɔ Benada, nanso wɔhwɛ kwan sɛ adɔkotafoɔ ne ayarehwɛfo bɛtua wɔn ka wɔ January 5 a ɛreba no mu.
Nanso aban asomfo bebree a wɔkasa kyerɛɛ Studio 7 no kaa sɛ wɔnnye nni sɛ wɔbɛnya wɔn sika no bio.
Yentumi nhuu Apɔmuden Soafoɔ, David Parirenyatwa ne Labor, Priscah Mupfumira, sɛ wɔnhwehwɛ akwan a wɔbɛfa so asiw atuatew ano.
Ɔsɔretia titiriw a ɛne MDC no anwiinwii sɛ polisifo rehaw emufo no.

Dr Nyampinga ka sɛ wɔbɛkɔ United States mmeae ahorow akosua afiase tebea ho ade sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wobetumi ahyɛ wɔn adwuma mu den wɔ fie.

Berɛ a ɔrekasa wɔ dwumadie no mu no, Ɔtwerɛtwerɛtwerɛtwerɛfoɔ a ɔhwɛ ma International Relations Michael Pompeo kaa sɛ adwuma a mmea 12 yɛ no yɛ hu, na ɛhia sɛ wonya akokoduru.
Wɔyɛɛ dwumadi no mfe 14 ni.
Afghanistan, Armenia, Azerbaijan, Bolivia, Burkino Faso, Kazakhstan, Malaysia, Nicaragua, Pakistan, Syria, Yemen ne Zimbabwe.
Owura Pompey kaa sɛ saa dwumadie yi ho hia paa bere a wɔmaa mmea nyaa hokwan yɛɛ adwuma maa nnipa a wɔwɔ wiase nyinaa no.
Ɔrekasa wɔ dwumadie no ase no, ɔbea a odi kan a ɔwɔ United States, Melania Trump, kae sɛ n’ani gyee hokwan a nnipa wɔ sɛ wɔyɛ adwuma a mmea reyɛ wɔ wiase nyinaa no ho.
Ɔkae sɛ efi bere a edi kan a wohyiaa mmea a wɔagye wɔn atom mfe anan a atwam ni no, wɔakɔ so ahyia mmea a wɔreyɛ adwuma a ɛyɛ anigye wɔ wiase nyinaa ɛmfa ho sɛ wɔn mu binom yɛ saa nnwuma yi na wɔteetee wɔn nanso wɔkɔ so yɛ no.
Dr Nyampinga ka sɛ ɔfii n’adwuma ase sɛ onipa a ɔwɔ hokwan sɛ ɔdi dwuma wɔ nnipa asetena mu mfeɛ 30 ni.

Nhwehwɛmu bi a wɔyɛe wɔ Zimbabwe a ɛwɔ China no da no adi sɛ ɛnyɛ. South Africa Asoɛe a ɛhwɛ Communicable Diseases so no wɔ nimdeɛ a ɛsen biara wɔ South Africa sɛ ɛbɛma wɔahu sɛ obi anya afunu no bi anaa.

Kwaadubɔ ne bɔs a ɛwɔ ZUPCO bɔs mu a wɔabara wɔn dwumadie no de ɔhaw abrɛ wɔn wɔ akwantuo ho, na ama nnipa a wɔrehyiam wɔ bɔs gyinabea bere a ɔman no repere sɛ wɔbɛtrɛw Covid-19 nsanyare mu wɔ ɔman no mu no.
Wɔka sɛ nnipa pii rehu amane wɔ karka mu, titiriw anwummere, na ɛma wɔn ho kyere wɔn wɔ bɔs kakra a ɛwɔ hɔ no mu.
Aban no ahyɛ mmara sɛ wɔn a wɔrebɛfa nnipa wɔ Covid-19 yareɛ yi mu no mfa wɔn ntu kwan mma wɔnsa yareɛ no, na wɔka sɛ ZUPCO nko ara na wɔma kwan ma wɔde bɔs fa nnipa.
Nanso wɔkyerɛ sɛ bɔs ne bɔs ahorow bi mpɛ sɛ wɔtwentwɛn wɔn nan ase wɔ nneɛma bi a ɛbɛma ZUPCO atua ka ho.
Wɔ Dwoda no, wɔbɔɔ amanneɛ sɛ nnipa a wɔwɔ bɔs mu no ne ZUPCO yɛɛ nhyiam bi de bɔɔ mmɔden sɛ wobedi wɔn haw no ho dwuma, a wɔn bɔs ka ho.
Benada no, na wɔhwɛ kwan sɛ bɔs no behyia aban mpanyimfo no ma wɔasiesie akasakasa no.

Adwumayɛfoɔ a wɔwɔ Bulawayo ne nkuropɔn mu nnwumakuo ahodoɔ ahyia akasa atia ɔhaw ahodoɔ a wɔsusu sɛ nsuo a wɔde di dwuma no de aba wɔn so no.

Owura Nyoni kaa sɛ aban mpanimfoɔ a wɔhyiaa no no ahyɛ no bɔ sɛ ɔbɛnya nsuo dapɛn a edi hɔ no ntɛm ara.
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ na Bulawayo kurow no adu ne dapɛn a ɛto so abien mu a na nsu nka ho bere a bagua no atu akɔ baabi a wɔrekosiesie nsu wɔ Criterion Water Works no.
Wɔka sɛ eyi nso fi nsubura a ɛwɔ kuropɔn no mu a ɛma Criterion ne Magwegwe ne Magwe a ɛwɔ ahoɔden a wɔde bɛsaw nsu no.
Owura Nyoni ka sɛ wonim no yiye sɛ Bulawayo kurow no adi boro mfe 120, na mfiri ne nsuka abu abɔ ho dedaw.

Owura Mnangagwa a na ɔrebetu kwan no san bae ntɛm ara sɛ ɔrebɛsɔ nnuruyɛfo no ahwɛ.

Zimbabwefoɔ bi a wɔwɔ South Africa akasa atia Groote Schuur Ayaresabea wɔ Cape Town, baabi a wɔresa Ɔmampanyin Constantino Chiwenga yareɛ no.
Wɔbɔɔ amanneɛ sɛ wɔbɔɔ Owura Chiwenga atuu fii ɔman no mu kɔɔ South Africa dapɛn awiei sɛ ɔrekɔsa ne ho yare. Ɛwom sɛ na Studio 7 ntumi nhu adanse biara a ɛkyerɛ sɛ ɔwɔ South Africa ayaresabea kɛse paa de.

Zimbabweni foforo a yɛfrɛ no Carlos Chimbi a ɔte Cape Town no de ne ho kɔbɔɔ Zimbabwefo a wɔyɛ saa atua no.
Chimbi kae sɛ na " ne werɛ ahow paa " sɛ ɔmampanyin abadiakyire no abu hokwan a nnipa wɔ wɔ ɔman no mu no so, efisɛ na onim sɛ sɛ ɔyare a, ɔbɛhwehwɛ ayaresa wɔ amannɔne.

Chimbi kaa sɛ ayaresabea hɔ panyin no aka akyerɛ no sɛ mmara mma no kwan sɛ ɔbɛka ayarefo a wɔbɛkɔ ayaresabea hɔ ho asɛm akyerɛ wɔn.

Bloomberg a wabɛyɛ ɔdefo pa no antu mmirika ankogyina n'afadie no ananmu wɔ abatoɔ mu, na Republican Amanyɔkuw no kasamafo Donald Trump nso bɛpene so.
Owura Bloomberg bɔɔ amanneɛ wɔ November afe a etwaam no mu sɛ ɔde ne ho rehyɛ apontow no ase, na ɔde sika bɛboro dɔla ɔpepem 400 rebɔ dawuru. Saa sika yi yɛ wɔn de.
Ɔdefo no anhyehyɛ mmara a ɛwɔ Iowa ne New Hampshire no, na saa ara nso na ɔrentu mmirika wɔ Navada ne South Carolina abatoɔ no mu bere a amantam 14 bɛpaw amammuo amammuo sɛ egyina Democratic Party ananmu wɔ US ɔmampanyin abatoɔ mu.
Bere a Bloomerg de ne nan sii fam wɔ adwuma no mu ara pɛ na wɔn a kan no na wɔyɛ adesuakuw no mufo te sɛ Bernie Sanders, a ogyina hɔ ma Mmarahyɛbɛdwani ne Elisabet a ogyina Massachusetts ananmu wɔ Senate no fii ase buu Bloomberg ho kyerɛwtohɔ no animtiaa.
Bere a Owura Sanders rekasa wɔ Nevada amanyɔkuo bi anim no, ɔkaa sɛ, ɛhia sɛ obi bɛtumi ateetee nnipa bebree wɔ Amerika abakɔsɛm mu sen bere biara.
Owura Sanders kaa sɛ, Owura Bloomberg yɛ obi a wagye din wɔ New York kuropɔn mu a ɔresi gyinae sɛ ɔbɛpɛ abibifo na wahwehwɛ wɔn, na afei nso wahwehwɛ Latinos, a ɔyɛɛ saa no. Ɔkae sɛ, saa kwan yi so no, nnipa rentumi ntu nnipa pii mma wɔntow aba mma Owura Trum no mfi hɔ wɔ November mu.
Nanso Bloomerg bɔɔ Owura Sanders asɛm no mua sɛ, Owura Sanders na wadi kan ato abadiakyire sɛ ɔde Democratic Party amammuo abadiakyire a ɔne Owura Trump bɛyɛ mfeɛ nnan a ɛdi hɔ no.
Amammui mu nhwehwɛmufo ne Zanu PF busuani, Frank Guni kaa no pefee sɛ akansi no da Sanders ne Bloomberg ntam, ɛwom sɛ na ɛda adi pefee sɛ seesei Sanders wɔ nnipa pii a wɔboaa wɔn ho dodo.

Bere a Jason Taylor rekasa akyerɛ Studio 7 wɔ US nnwumayɛbea no, USAID dwumayɛni a ɔda asiane ano no kae sɛ bere a wɔne nnwumakuo foforo reyɛ adwuma de asiesie adan a asɛe no, wɔde wɔn adwene sii aduane so sɛ ɛbɛma nnipa anya nkwa.

Taylor, a ɔkɔɔ Manicaland mantam mu a ɔda Wiase Aduan Ho Dwumadie a ɛwɔ helicopter ano no kaa sɛ, ne ho dwiriw no sɛ ohuu sɛnea nkurɔfo ho yeraw wɔn wɔ ɔmantam no mu.
Ɔkae sɛ mmofra a ohuu wɔn no nni anigye. Ɔkae sɛ ɛho hia sɛ nnipa a wɔwɔ Manicaland no nya nneɛma te sɛ aduan ne dabere mu mfaso akyi no, ɛsɛ sɛ wɔboa wɔn nso ma wɔsan hyehyɛ wɔn ntade.
Taylor san kae sɛ wɔ Chimanimani ne Chipinge no, wɔanhu ahɔho a wɔkaa sɛ wɔremmoa wɔn wɔ amanyɔkuo a wɔgyina wɔn akyi no.

Ayarefo bi ka sɛ wɔresɔ wɔn ahwɛ wɔ amannɔne bere a ayarehwɛfo bi a wɔka sɛ wosuro sɛ wobetumi awu wɔ ayaresabea a wɔmma wɔn ayaresa no asiw wɔn kwan no.
Nhwehwɛmu bi a Studio 7 ayɛ no ada no adi sɛ ayarefo bi retu kwan akɔ aman foforo te sɛ South Africa, Botswana ne Zambia akɔsa akɔsa wɔn yareɛ wɔ hɔ.
Ayarefo a yɛne wɔn kasae wɔ Parirenyatwa mu no mu baako a wɔfrɛ no Ms Molline Chindove kaa sɛ waba ayaresabea hɔ nna pii nanso biribiara ankɔ yiye.
Ms Chindove kaa sɛ ɔrekɔ South Africa akɔsa ne nan a ɛwɔ nsu no mu no yareɛ nti.

Nhwehwɛmu bi a Studio 7 ayɛ no ada no adi sɛ nnipa bebree a wɔtoo wɔn paa wɔ ayaresabea hɔ no rehwehwɛ ayaresa a ɛbɛma ɔmanfoɔ ayarehwɛ.
Wilbert Kasanze kae sɛ ɔde ne yere fii Chegutu General Ayaresabea kɔɔ ayaresabea bi wɔ Chitungwiza.
Kasanze ka sɛ da biara bɔs a efi Chegutu kɔ Chitungwiza no ama ne kotoku mu sika a ɔde betu mmirika.

Wɔn a wɔda so ara pɛ adwuma no nso hyɛɛ wɔn sɛ wɔnsan mfi adwuma no ase na wɔnhyɛ wɔn nkuran sɛ wɔnsan nyɛ adwuma no bio.

Abenfo Fekubɔfo Priscilla Mangwiro a ɔwɔ Zimbabwe no kae sɛ ɛho hia sɛ nkurɔfo kɔ oduruyɛfo a ɔfata hɔ bere a wɔwɔ ɔhaw no.

Ms. Mangwiro ka sɛ efi October 1, bere a wɔyɛɛ Kokoram adwuma sɛ Cancer Adwuma wɔ Month no, n'ahyehyɛde no asɔ mmea bɛboro 50 ahwɛ, na wɔn dodow bɛkɔ soro akodu ɔsram yi awiei.

Ms Mangwiro ka sɛ nneɛma pii wɔ hɔ a ɛma mmea nya nufu mu kokoram.

Ms Mangwiro ka sɛ nnipa pii susuw sɛ kokoram a wohu no kyerɛ sɛ wɔrewuwu, nanso nneɛma pii wɔ hɔ a wobetumi ayɛ de aboa mmea ma wɔanyin akyɛ.
Ms . Mangwiro ka sɛ ade baako a ɛde kokoram ba ne aduan a srade ne asikre pii wom a wodi.
Ms. Mangwiro rehyɛ mmea nkuran sɛ wɔmfa October hokwan a ɛbɛma wɔatumi asɔ kokoram ahwɛ no nni dwuma, na wɔnkyerɛkyerɛ yare no ho ade.

Zimbabweans on Memeneda da a ɛtɔ so 40 no, ɔman no ahofadi ne abibifo ne abibifo foforo de wɔn ayɛ nkoa.
Abibifo akuturukubɔ no maa nnipa pii nyaa anidaso sɛ awiei koraa no, wobenya dibea a ɛkorɔn, a aborɔfo de wɔn mu pii agu bun no mu bere a wɔfaa wɔn asase pa no nyinaa kɔe no.

Chiwenga a wɔyɛɛ no adwadie mu sɛ ɔmmma aban no ne dɔkotafoɔ no ntam kwan nnyɛ adwuma.
Nnipa pii a wɔka sɛ Owura Chiwenga de sraadi ho nsɛm a ɛhia sɛ wɔka ho asɛm no akasa atia wɔn nneyɛe no.
Adɔkotafoɔ ka sɛ wɔpɛ sɛ aban no ma wɔn nnuruyɛ, nnuruyɛ ne ntade a ɛbɛbɔ wɔn ho ban bere a wɔreyɛ adwuma no, na saa ara nso na wɔpɛ sɛ wɔnya sika pii te sɛ towtua.
Nanso aban no ka sɛ ne kɔfe no asɛe araa ma ɛrentumi nyɛ yiye.
Yentumi nte akwahosan soafo panin, Owura Obadia Moyo, bere a ntɛm ara ɔne oduruyɛfo a ɔhwɛ yare no kɔɔ nhyiam bere a edi kan wɔ wimhyɛn mu no.
Labor Asɛnnibea no ampene so sɛ aban no mpene nkrataa biara a ɛwɔ ho no so, efisɛ ɛtia dɔktafoɔ a wɔrenyɛ adwuma.
Doug Coltart, mmaranimfoɔ a ɔgyina Zimbabwe Ayaresabea Fekuw a ɛwɔ Labor Court no anim no kaa sɛ ɛnni krataa biara a ɛbɛtumi afi Apɔmuden Asoeɛ Board, HSB hɔ, enti wɔantumi ante asɛm no wɔ mmara mu.
Asɛnnibea no hyɛɛ HSB mmaranimfo no sɛ wɔnhyehyɛ nkrataa a ayera no ɔkyena, Wukuda.
Nanso adɔkotafoɔ aka sɛ, sɛ wobɛkɔ asɛnnibea a, ɛnyɛ ɛno na ɛbɛma wɔatumi akɔ adwuma, enti ɛrenni ɔhaw no ho dwuma.
Aguadikuo a ɛwɔ Zimbabwe Ayaresabea Ntam Nkitahodifoɔ, Doctor Masimba Ndoro kaa sɛ n’adwuma no hwehwɛ sɛ ɔde ne ho hyɛ adwuma mu da biara da, na ehia sɛ wɔtua no ka wɔ eyi ho.
Dɔktafoɔ no bɔɔ adwadifoɔ no sɛ wɔnni sika pii a wɔde bɛyɛ adwuma.
Dɔktafoɔ a wɔwɔ Zimbabwe Senior Ayaresabea Fekuw mu no nso bɔɔ hu Yawo da a etwaam no, na wonwiinwii wɔ akatua pa ne nnuruyɛ mu ayaresa ho.
Nnuruyɛfo a wɔn mfe akɔ anim no nso kyerɛw krataa de nwiinwii faa ahunahuna a na wɔrefa mu no ho, na wɔkae sɛ anyɛ yiye sɛ nnuruyɛfo bɛkɔ ayaresabea ahorow a wonni nneɛma a ɛfata a wɔde begye ayarefo nkwa.
Nnuruyɛfo no kasa tiaa aban no, na wɔkae sɛ sika no akɔ soro ɔha mu nkyem 60, na wɔka sɛ wɔne no nyɛ adwene.
Saa bere yi mu no, nnuruyɛfo baanu a wɔn mfe akɔ anim abɔ mmɔden sɛ wobetua wɔn ka wɔ Zimbabwe Sukuupɔn mu sɛ wɔmfa wɔn ho nhyɛ atuateɛ no mu na

Moyo kaa sɛ aban no retwɛn nea ɛrekɔ so wɔ asɛnnibea hɔ no, na ɛno akyi no ɔkaa tebea no ho asɛm kyerɛɛ wɔn.

Owura Muchichwa nso kaa sɛ, sɛ wɔkyere wɔn a wɔsesa sika no a, wɔrentumi nni ɔhaw no ho dwuma te sɛ nea wɔbɛyɛ no nna kakraa bi, na afei wɔasan afi wɔn dwumadi no ase.
Sikasɛm ho dwumadie no agye atom sɛ, sɛ yɛde sika a yɛde bɛma akwahosan ho dwumayɛni no toto akwahosan ho nsɛnnennen a ɛwɔ hɔ seesei no ho a, ɛbɛkɔ so atu mpɔn.

Nanso kan sikasɛm soafo Tendai Biti, a ɔyɛ MDC-T kannifo baasa no mu biako ka sɛ, ɔman no sikasɛm mu ahokyere reyɛ kɛse bere a ɔman no sikakorabea atitiriw, Reserve Bank of Zimbabwe no reyɛ nneɛma pii sen sɛnea anka ɛsɛ sɛ ɔman no bɔ ka no.
Owura Biti nso a ɔhwɛ abɛɛfo sikasɛm ho dwumadie so no kaa sɛ, sikasɛm ntotoeɛ no ne sikakorabea kɛseɛ no mfa mmara a ɛwɔ ɔman no sikasɛm mu no nyɛ adwuma.
Nanso ɛsɛ sɛ amanfoɔ hu sɛ mfeɛ bebree ni a ɔman no sika a ɛnnye mfɛntom wɔ ɔman no dan mu, enti ɛgye berɛ ansa na ɔhaw no aba.

Awarefo hwe wɔn wia ade de kunkum wɔn ho

" Mesan kɔtraa mpɔtam hɔ.

Seesei, asomdwoe wɔ hɔ.
Abarimaa no nni hɔ, ɔbea no wɔ hɔ.
Meda so ara rehwehwɛ n'abusua, na yɛne wɔn behyiam ɔkyena (benn) asusuw asɛm no ho, " Ngubobo.
KwaZulu-Natal polisifo kasamafo Captain Nqobile Gwala kaa sɛ nnipa baanu a wɔadi awu abue wɔn ano, na polisifo da so ara rehwehwɛ wɔn a wɔsusu sɛ wɔadi wɔn awu no.
Mmɔden a Solezwe bɔe sɛ ɔbɛhwehwɛ wɔn a wɔakunkum wɔn no mmusua mu no anyɛ yiw, efisɛ na wɔn dodow nni hɔ nkosi bere a nsɛm ho amanneɛbɔfo de wɔn ho hyem.
Ná Guptafo no de sika gu sikakorabea ahorow
AFRICAN NEWS AGENCY (ANA) bu akontaa sɛ ɔman no kyerɛɛ R49 sɛ ɔman no ani ansɔ nnipa ɔpepepem pii no, sɛnea Shadow World kwankyerɛfo Paul Edward Holden kyerɛ no.
Ɔpanyin no kaa saa asɛm yi wɔ dwumadie bi a Ɔtemmufo Raymond Zondo de sii hɔ nnɛra.

Ná wɔtaa de 68 gu sikakorabea ahorow.

Holden bisabisaa Advocate Matthew Chaskalson nsɛm.
Holden ka kyerɛɛ wɔn sɛ n'adansedi no gyina amanneɛbɔ ne sika a wɔde maa Gupta nnwuma so.
Ɔkyerɛe sɛ Guptas no hwiee R287 guu Estina Dairy Farm Project so.
Na nhyehyɛe no ne sɛ wɔbɛyɛ akuafo wɔ Free State.
Holden kaa sɛ, Gupta no fii ase wiaa sika afe baako ansa na Estina dwumadi no refi ase.
Aban a ɛwɔ Free State no fii ase de sika hyɛɛ Estina dwumadie no mu wɔ June 2011 mu nanso Guptas fii ase de sika guu dwumadie no mu wɔ May 2011 mu.
"They de Estina nhyehyɛe no dii dwuma de sika siee sum ase, ansa na dwumadi no refi ase" Holden kaa sɛ.
Sɛnea amanneɛbɔ no kyerɛ no, aban no tuaa R287 ka kyerɛɛ Gupta abusua no, na wɔde sika no hyɛɛ adwumakuw no sikasɛm mu na ama ayɛ te sɛ nea na ɛreyɛ adwuma wɔ afe 2012 ne afe 2016 ntam no.

Wɔkyerɛ sɛ biribi pa bi sii wɔ IFP mantam no mu wɔ Melmoth
Wɔbɔɔ IFP councilors sobo sɛ wabɔ n'awɛmfo a wɔbɔɔ wɔn tuo piraa nnipa baasa wɔ nhyiam bi ase wɔ Thubalethu, Mthonjane (Melmoth), Kwasida awia.
Wɔka sɛ Kɔtɔnimfoɔ no de anamɔn a wɔbɔɔ nnipakuo a ɛwɔ hɔ a wɔse bha· monarch too nhyiam asa no ano no so.
Ɔman no fã bi bɔɔ amanyɔkuo no kannifo soboɔ sɛ wabɔ mmɔden sɛ ɔde wɔn kotodwe bɛma wɔn nkotodwe bere a wɔhyɛɛ wɔn sɛ wɔnsan nkɔ mansini bi a ɛwɔ IFP-
IFP kannifo a ɔwɔ Ɔhene Cetshwayo mantam mu no frɛɛ nhyiam no sɛ wɔnkyerɛ ɔsɛmpɔw a ahye ɔman no mu no mu, bere a dapɛn a etwaam no ɔsɔre tiaa asɔfo a wɔpam wɔn no nyinaa, a wɔn a kan na wɔyɛ Bonginkosi Biyela ka ho.
Ɔmanfoɔ no mu baako a ɔdii atua wɔ tuo no ho a na ɔmpɛ sɛ wɔde ne din bɛto no so no bɔɔ no soboɔ sɛ, IFP kannifo ne asɔfoɔ no denam awɛmfoɔ a ɔbɔɔ wɔn soboɔ sɛ wɔbɛtumi abɔ wɔn tuo na amma wɔn bo amfuw wɔn.
" NAWe rekasa wɔ abɔnten so efisɛ na wɔmma yɛn kwan mma yɛnkɔ asa no so efisɛ na nnipa a wɔwɔ mmeae foforo ahyɛ so mã.
Ɔhaw no fii ase bere a yɛkyeree ɔmanfoɔ a na wɔrebɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛhyɛ no ma wafa ɔkwan a emu yɛ den so, na awɛmfoɔ ne apaafo a wɔwɔ hɔ no nyaa kwan sɛ wɔbɛtow tuo no. "
IFP kannifo a ɔwɔ Mthonjaneni a ɔmpɛ sɛ yɛto no din no kaa sɛ nnipa a wɔwɔ mpɔtam hɔ no mu apaapae.
" Nnawɔtwe biara no, wɔyɛɛ kyenkyenee bi de kyerɛe sɛ wɔmpene so sɛ wɔbɛpam wɔn nua no afi ne nsam.
Wɔayɛ nhyiam ho nhyehyɛe ama asafo mu mpanyimfo ne IFP mantam mu mpanyimfo nyinaa sɛ wɔmma ɔmanfo no aduan.
" Ɔhaw no fii ase bere a na ɔmanfo no bi gyinagyina asa no akyi no, na nhyiam no fii ase, na bere a nhyiam no fii ase no, wosiw kwan a ɛda asa no ano, abo a wɔde abɔ wɔn ho ban na wɔhyɛɛ wɔn ma wɔtotow atuo efisɛ na ɔmanfo no retow ahyɛ wɔn so.
Ɔmanfo no bi de tuo kyerɛɛ wɔn. "

Krataa bi wɔ m’adwumam.

Yei dapɛn yi mu no aban atu anamɔn yi so de ato dwa sɛ wabue kwan ama Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie Kwankyerɛfoɔ panin a ɔfiri Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie ase afɛm Zimbabwean dɔla ɔpepem 388.
Bere a Interior Minister Kazembe Kazembe Kazembe rekasa akyerɛ nsɛntwerɛfoɔ no, ɔkaa sɛ n’adwafie no yɛ akwanhwɛ pa a nnipa betumi afa so anya wɔn hyɛn gyinabea no ntɛm ara, ne sɛ, nnipa a wɔrebɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔde nkrataa yi bɛkɔ amannɔne no, ne titiriw no, nkrataa apa ho.
Kazembe kaa sɛ ɔbɛma aman foforo anya mmara ho nkrataa wɔ wɔn man mu, aban no ahu sɛ ɛfata sɛ ɔma boɔ no so, na wɔde saa nkrataa yi bɛma no ntɛm ara.
Nanso ebinom a wɔatu wɔn ho no te nka sɛ aban no ayɛ nhyehyɛe a ɛbɛma ɔman foforo agye wɔn ho.
Sɛ wɔkyem pɛpɛɛpɛ a, hyɛn gyinabea dwumayɛni a ɔwɔ ɔman no mu tua $ 53 ma RTGS no, na nea ɔpɛ sɛ ofi hɔ no tua $ 250.

Paradza kaa sɛ nnipa bebree a wɔatu kwan aba hɔ ate sɛ wɔn busuani ne wɔn nnamfo akyɛ ade, na wotuaa sika akɛse maa wɔn akwantu tumi nkrataa.
Isaac Nyaumba a ofi Zimbabwean man mu no kaa sɛ n’ani gyei sɛ onyaa hokwan hyiaa bɔɔlbɔni a wagye din Neymar na otwaa no mfonini.
Neymar a wɔwoo no wɔ Sao Paulo, Brazil, na ne din nyinaa yɛ Neymar da Silva Santos Júnior.
Seesei Neymar redi agoru ama Barcelona ne bɔɔlbɔ kuw foforo, Lionel Messi. Ɔno nso dii agoru maa Brazil, na ɔde sika kɔkɔɔ abasobɔde no kɔɔ Olympics.
Nanso ɛwom sɛ nnipa pii ka sɛ woyii Nyaumba ne Neymar mfonini no adi wɔ Victoria Aworoeɛ mu de, nanso wɔka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ wɔyɛɛ no bere a na ɔreyɛ adwuma wɔ Ukutula Conservation Center a ɛbɛn Pretoria wɔ South Africa no.
Mighty Warriors mmea bɔɔlbɔ kuw no rehyia apereperedi kɛse bi wɔ n’abakɔsɛm mu, na amamfrafoɔ a wɔwɔ Zimbabwe no adi nkonim wɔ ɔman no agumadi mu.
Mighty Warrier no rehyɛn Rufaro Agumadibea Kwasida wɔ wɔn akansi kɛse no mu fi 1980 bere a Zimbabwe fii amanaman ntam akansi ase no.
Mmea a wɔyɛ bɔɔlbɔ kuw no rehyia Indomitable Lionesses of Cameroon wɔ akansi bi mu a ɛbɛma wɔahu sɛ ebia Zimbabwe betumi afata ama Olimpik Games in Rio de Janeiro afe a ɛreba no.
Wɔboroo Mightight Warrier no 2 - 1 bere a akuw abien no hyiae wɔ Yaounde adapɛn abien a atwam no, nanso wɔn mu 1 pɛ na wohia na wɔatumi afata ama Wiase Nyinaa Adesuakuw no.
Aguadifoɔ panin panin panin panin, Mighty Warriors de ayɛ adwuma mfeɛ aduonum sɛ ɔbɛsi akan wɔ amansini a ɛwɔ afe 1980 akyi no mu.
Nanso Mighty Warriors nkɔɔ so wɔ abakɔsɛm mu bere a wɔn a wodii kan bɔɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛsi akan wɔ amansini dwumadi mu bere a wɔtoo nsa frɛɛ mmeawa a wɔde wɔn rekɔ Moscow bere a wɔtoo nsa frɛɛ wɔn sɛ wɔmmra amansini no mu no.
Warriors Fan Kuw no muni, Zivanai Moroyiwa, ka sɛ wɔretwentwɛn wɔn nan ase wɔ agodie no ho sɛ, Mighty Warriors no bɛma ɔmanfo ani agye denam nea kuw no anaa kuw biara anyɛ wɔ mfe 35 a atwam no mu no so.
Caps United panin Tonderayi Matimura ka sɛ, sɛ kuw abien no hyiam adapɛn abien a atwam no a, wɔwɔ ahotoso sɛ Might Warriors no bedi nkonim bio.
Zimbabwe Football Association ahu hia a ɛho hia sɛ ɔmanfo di agoru no, na wayɛ nhyehyɛe ama ɔmanfoɔ no tua sika a wɔde bɛhwɛ agodie a ɛho hia yi.

Owura Matimura kae sɛ ɔmmra agoprama yi so sɛ ɔdeduani no yɛ sika a ne bo yɛ den sen dɔla abiɛsa a Zifa frɛ no.
Abɛdreck Mlauzi bɔɔlbɔkuo no ahyɛ adwadifoɔ ne wɔn a wɔn aso yɛ den, na ɔhwɛ kwan sɛ wɔn a wɔdi agorɔ te sɛ Rudo Nesham ne Rutendo Machingura de gya besi hɔ Kwasida wɔ wɔn akyitaafoɔ anim.
Bere koro no ara mu no, Warriors kuw no bɛwɔ Bourfields Stadium a wɔne Lesotho wɔ African Nations Champion akansie a ne mu duru nnu Might Warriors akansie no.
Kalisto Pasuwa bɔɔ bɔɔlbɔfoɔ baasa Hardlife Zvirei ne Justice Jangano a ɔwɔ Caps United ne Ronald Chitiyo a ɔwɔ Dynamos a wɔde wɔn ho hyɛ nna mu ɔbrasɛe mu nanso Muroyiwa kaa sɛ Akodifo no annyae akuo nketewa te sɛ Lesotho.
Akodifoɔ no rehwɛ kwan sɛ wɔbɛdi akuo mmienu yi so nkonim na ama awieɛ yi dwumadie a ɛtwa toɔ wɔ akuo mmienu yi mu no akɔ awieɛ wɔ afe a ɛtɔ so anan mu wɔ afe 2009, 2012 ne afe 2014 mu.

Abɔnten so adwadifoɔ a wɔwɔ Harare ne Tajamuka / Sesijikile adwadifoɔ abɛdi ako atia kuropɔn mu polisifo ne Zimbabwe Republic Polisifoɔ a wɔbɔɔ amanneɛ sɛ wɔayi wɔn afi wɔn nnwuma mu no.
Saa ara na esii wɔ Norton kurow mu, baabi a wɔbɔɔ amanneɛ sɛ mmɔnten so aguadifo no ampene so bere a wɔretɔn wɔ Katanga no.
Tajamuka / Sesijikile kasamafoɔ, Makomborero Haruzivishe kaa sɛ n’adwumakuo no mufo bi yɛ n’adwumakuo a polisifo taa teetee wɔn.
Haruzivishe kaa sɛ bere a yɛkɔɔ wimhyɛn mu no, yɛda so ara wɔ polisifo adwumayɛbea hɔ sɛ yɛbɛhwɛ nnipa dodow a wɔakyere wɔn wɔ asɛm yi mu, nanso ɔkaa sɛ wonim wɔn mu baako.
Harare City Bagua no kasamafo Michael Chideme kae sɛ wɔntee asɛm no bere a na wɔntee asɛm no wɔ kurow no mu saa da no.
Nanso aban no nam Information Ministry of Information so de nkrasɛm bi too Twitter anim sɛ polisifo asiw mmabun pii abo akum wɔn.
Aban no aka sɛ ɛwɔ video so adanseɛ a ɛkyerɛ sɛ mmofra a wɔadu mpanyin afe so no hyɛ polisifoɔ nsa, na wɔde bɛdi dwuma wɔ asɛnnibea de atuateɛ no.
Yentumi ntee asɛm no mfii polisifo hɔ.
Zimbabwe Community a ɛwɔ South Africa, ahyehyɛde a egyina hɔ ma Zimbabweanfo a wɔte hɔ na wɔyɛ adwuma wɔ South Africa no, ka sɛ akorɔmfoɔ a wɔwɔ Johannesburg borɔn bi so a wɔn a wosusuw sɛ Zimbabweanfo na wodi wɔn nsɛmmɔne no ho asɛm hia wɔn paa.
Kuw no ka sɛ, nsɛmmɔne a wodi wɔ Hillbrow, Berea ne Yeoville titiriw ne aman foforo pii, a Zimbabweanfo, a wɔn a wɔkyere nkurɔfo sie, wɔn a wɔkyere wɔn sie, ne awudifo ka ho.
Zimbabwe Community a ɛwɔ South Africa no kasamafo Bongani Mtuanzi kaa sɛ wɔyɛɛ nhyehyɛe sɛ wɔne polisifo behyia asɛm no, na wahyɛ polisifo nkuran sɛ wɔnyɛ biribi a anibere wom.
Ɔkaa sɛ February 6, a ɛbɛkɔ so bosome a ɛdi hɔ no, n’ahyehyɛde no rehwɛ kwan sɛ wɔne polisifoɔ a wɔwɔ amansin no mu bɛbom ayɛ adwuma de adi ɔhaw no ho dwuma.
Wɔka nso sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ polisifo kyinkyin mpɔtam hɔ, nanso mpɛn pii no wontumi nyɛ ho hwee, ɛno na ɛbɛma akorɔmfo ne adwowtwafoɔ a wɔyɛ Jojina ne ne yere aka.

Ɔkaa saa asɛm yi kyerɛɛ Sikasɛm Soafoɔ, Owura Ken Ofori-Attah bɛboa ɔne Ghanafoɔ ma wɔakɔ so abɔ adwadeɛ yi ho nkɔmmɔ.
“Mahu sɛ asɛmmisa no ne sɛ mɛhunu sɛ ɔman yi boɔ a ɛsii afe 2013 kosi 2017 berɛ a Ɔmanpanin Mahama de wimhyɛn tu kwan toatoa so no.”
Ahosiesie a ɛte saa ara
Bere a Owura Barimah de n’adwene sii n’adwenkyerɛ a ɛbɛma wabua asɛmmisa a ɛho hia a ɛwɔ Kasamafo Adwumayɛbea hɔ so no, ɔkaa n’asɛmmisa no wɔ amanyɔsɛm mu.
“Yei ara na yɛsii gyinaeɛ sɛ ɔman yi retu anamɔn bi na yɛresi gyinaeɛ yie berɛ a yɛnim sɛ saa asɛm no yɛ adwuma a ɛsɛ sɛ yɛnya firi nea yɛayɛ dedaw no mu.
“Haa na wadi kan ayɛ adwuma? Na sɛ anim wɔ hɔ a, dɛn na na wɔyɛ? Na so ɔkwankyerɛfo bi wɔ hɔ a ɔfa so tu kwan kɔ ɔmampanyin kwan yi so? Enti ɛda adi pefee sɛ mempɛ sɛ menya amanyɔsɛm biara a ɛte saa.
Ɔde kaa ho sɛ, “Mepɛ sɛ yenya anobaabaeɛ pa ne ɔkasa ho na ama yɛatumi atwe nsɛm a ɛfata ato hɔ nnɛ, ɛyɛ m’aban nanso ɔkyena ɛbɛyɛ aban, enti sɛ yɛanhwehwɛ nkyerɛkyerɛmu papa, na yɛantwa akwantuo yi so a, yɛbɛkɔ so anya yɛn ho wɔ saa tebea yi mu.”
Ablakwa bisaa asɛm a ɛho hia paa

“Mehoahoa me ho na m’ani agye paa sɛ mihui sɛ NPP ne NDC a ɛwɔ Bono Apuei fam no reyɛ adwuma asomdwoe mu de asiesie amanyɔsɛm a ɛwɔ wɔn ntam no.”
Owura Adu-Gyan kaa sɛ asomdwoe maa nneɛma kɔɔ so yiye, na ɔde kaa ho sɛ, sɛ asomdwoe nni hɔ a, ɛbɛyɛ den ama ɔman yi mu.

Ɔman Asomdwoe Bagua no de dwumadie a ɛfiri Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie a ɛtɔ so dummiɛnsa no too dwa sɛ: “Sɛnea Post 2020 Election Violence, ne Consensus for Greater Political Tolerance wɔ Ghana”
Nsɛmma nhoma no kaa asɛnhia bi a wɔde di dwuma wɔ abatoɔ ne akasamu ne nsɛmnsɛm a ɛfa abatoɔ ne akasakasa ho.

Ɔmaa wɔn awerɛhyem sɛ Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu Mmarahyɛbɛdwafifoɔ (RC) bɛhwɛ ama asomdwoeɛ a ɛhia sɛ wɔnya nkɔsoɔ no aba.

“Ɔmanfira a wɔde bɛbu atɛn, ɛwom sɛ ɛnyɛ ade foforɔ de, nanso wɔabu no sɛ ɛyɛ ade titiriw a ama nnipa nneyɛe gu ahorow, sɛ́ ɛyɛ adapaa anaa nhyehyɛeɛ no.”
Alhaji Quandah sii so dua sɛ ɛho hia sɛ wɔtĩ ɔman no atemmu nhyehyɛe mu bere ne bere mu na ama awie n’adwuma a ɛbɛma wɔatumi atow aba a ntease nnim na ɛfata.
Mmarahyɛbɛdwani a ɔwɔ Abuakwa Kesee fam Samuel Atta Akyea no ama Ghanafoɔ a ɔda Nana Akufo-Addo-Addo aban mu no anya wɔn tebea no so tumi fi January 7, 2017.

“Yanuary 7 bɛyɛ bere foforɔ a ɛde yɛn yiyedi ne yɛn ahofadi bɛba, ɛnkanka sikasɛm mu ahofadie a Ghanafoɔ rehwehwɛ no. Ghanafoɔ bɛkɔ akohu sɛ Onyankopɔn agye ɔman no afi ahokyere mu” Atta Apapa a ɔde ama Asiakwa SOS wɔ East Akimnicipity a ɛwɔ Apuei fam mantam mu.
Ɔkaa sɛ wayɛ krado sɛ ɔbɛsom wɔ asafo mu sɛ Ɔmanpanin abɛdiakyire Nana Akuffo-Addo de no bɛma no.
Nneɛma a ɔde mae no bi ne ɛmo ason, ngo, nkyene, nufusu, ne nufusu, ne sika a ne bo nyɛ den.

Anuanom baasa no wuwui wɔ frigye mu.

Ɔkaa sɛ ɔne n’asraafoɔ no de mmirika kɔɔ nanso wɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ Abena Amos, Arabi Dadzi, 13 ne Akaba Dadzi na wadi mfeɛ 7 wɔ Tarkwa Aban Ayaresabea hɔ retwɛn otwa yareɛ bi.
Bere a Starr News Emmanuel Ohene Gyankyi bisabisaa no nsɛm no, ɔkaa sɛ nea wawu no ne wɔn maame na ɛte, na ɔno na ɔyɛ ‘Golden City Kitchen City Kitchen a ɛwɔ Tara Nsuem mantam mu no mu adwuma.
Ɔkae sɛ wosii gyinae sɛ wobetwa anadwo wɔ asanombea hɔ bere a wɔboaa wɔn maame ma ɔtɔn nneɛma no.

Bere a Owura Mahamafo rekasa wɔ Tarkwa-suaem wɔ Atɔeɛ Mantam mu no, ɔdwenee nea enti a Akuffo-Addo aban no ani nnye ho sɛ ɔbɛda ne suban pa a ɛwɔ NAM1 ho adi na mmom ɔde wɔn bo befuw wɔn adetɔfo no ho.
“Nea ɛda nsow wɔ NAM 1 ho araa ma Akufo-Addo rebɔ ne ho ban? Dɛn nti na moma polisifo a wɔn ho nni asɛm no ho kwan bere a NAM 1 nantew kwa no.
